[\[1b.1\]{D4099}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_u dAn brga/_bod skad du/_ched du brjod pa'i tshoms/_bam po dang po/_thams cad mkhyen pa la phyag 'tshal lo/_/bkra shis par gyur
[\[1b.2\]]cig_/rgyal bas ched du brjod gsungs pa/_/bdag gis rab tu bshad par bya/_/gnyid dang rmugs pa rnams sol la/_/yid la dga' ba bskyed de nyon/_/thams cad mkhyen pa skyob
[\[1b.3\]]pa po/_/thub pa chen po thugs brtse ba/_/sku yi tha ma 'dzin pa'i tshe/_/bcom ldan 'das kyis 'di skad gsungs/_/kye ma 'dus byas rnams mi rtag_/skye zhing 'jig pa'i chos
[\[1b.4\]]can yin/_/skyes nas 'jig par 'gyur ba ste/_/de dag nye bar zhi ba bde/_/de ltar rab tu 'bar ba la/_/ci zhig dgar yod mgur ci yod/_/mun pa'i nang zhugs gnas pa dag_/
[\[1b.5\]]ci phyir sgron ma tshol mi byed/_/rus pa thi ba'i mdog 'dra ba/_/bor ba gang yin 'di dag ni/_/phyogs dang phyogs su rnam 'thor ba/_/de mthong 'di la ci zhig dga'/_/gang gi nub mo
[\[2a\]]
[\[2a.1\]]kho na nas/_/mngal du dang por zhugs pa'i mi/_/de ni sdod med 'gror 'gyur zhing /_/song ba las kyang ldog pa med/_/snga dro skye bo mang mthong ba/_/phyi dro kha cig mthong mi 'gyur/_/phyi dro skye bo mang
[\[2a.2\]]mthong ba/_/snga dro kha cig mthong mi 'gyur/_/skyes pa bud med mang po dang /_/dar la bab pa'ang 'chi 'gyur na/_/de la mi 'di gzhon zhes te/_/gson pa'i gdeng drod ci zhig yod/_/kha cig mngal du 'chi bar
[\[2a.3\]]'gyur/_/de bzhin kha cig btsas pa'i sar/_/de bzhin kha cig gog tsam la/_/de bzhin kha cig yongs rgyug na/_/la la rgan dang la la gzhon/_/la la dar la bab pa'i mi/_/rim gyis rab tu 'gro 'gyur te/_/
[\[2a.4\]]'bras bu smin pa ltung 'gyur bzhin/_/dper na 'bras bu smin pa rnams/_/lhung bas rtag tu 'jigs pa ltar/_/de bzhin skyes par gyur pa'i mi/_/rtag tu 'chi bas 'jigs par 'gyur/_/dper na rdza ma'i
[\[2a.5\]]mkhan po yis/_/'jim pa las ni snod byas pa/_/thams cad tha mar 'jig pa ltar/_/mi rnams srog kyang de bzhin no/_/dper na thags ni brkyang ba la/_/spun ni gang dang gang bcug pa'i/_/spun gyis
[\[2b\]]
[\[2b.1\]]rting la gtugs pa ltar/_/mi rnams srog kyang de bzhin no/_/dper na nges par gsad pa dag_/gom pa gang dang gang bor bas/_/bsad sa'i drung du bsnyen pa ltar/_/mi rnams srog kyang de bzhin no/_/chu klung brag tu 'bab pa'i rgyun/_/ldog pa med pa ji lta bar/_/de bzhin
[\[2b.2\]]mi yi tshe 'gro ba/_/slar ni ldog par 'gyur ba med/_/dka' ba nyid dang thung ba dang /_/de yang sdug bsngal ldan pa dag_/myur ba kho nar 'jig 'gyur te/_/chu la dbyu gus bris pa bzhin/_/dper na phyugs rdzi dbyug thogs kyis/_/phyugs rnams gnas su phyin byed ltar/_/de
[\[2b.3\]]bzhin nad dang rga ba yis/_/mi rnams 'chi bdag drung du skyel/_/chu bran gyi ni chu lta bur/_/nyin dang mtshan mo 'das pa yis/_/mi rnams tshe yang zad 'gyur zhing /_/srog kyang nye bar 'jig par 'gyur/_/mel tshe byed la mtshan mo ring /_/lam gyis du ba la rgyang grags ring /_/
[\[2b.4\]]dam chos rnam par mi shes pa'i/_/byis pa rnams la 'khor ba ring /_/bdag la bu yod de bzhin du/_/nor yod ces pas byis pa brlag_/phyi rol nang na bdag med na/_/su yi bu yin ci zhig nor/_/skyes pa bud med rnams kyi rigs/_/brgya dang stong phrag mang po dang /_/longs
[\[2b.5\]]spyod legs par bsgrubs pa yang /_/'chi bdag dbang du 'gro bar 'gyur/_/bsags pa kun gyi mtha' zad cing /_/bslang ba'i mtha' ni 'gyel bar 'gyur/_/phrad pa'i mtha' ni 'bral ba ste/_/gson pa'i mtha' ni 'chi ba yin/_/gson mtha' 'chi ba yin pas na/_/
[\[2b.6\]]sems can thams cad 'chi 'gyur zhing /_/dge sdig 'bras bur nyer 'gro ba'i/_/ji bzhin las kyi rjes su 'brang /_/sdig pa'i las kyis dmyal ba dang /_/bsod nams byas pas bde 'gro ste/_/gzhan dag gis ni lam bsgoms pas/_/zag med mya ngan 'das par 'gyur/_/
[\[2b.7\]]gang yang sangs rgyas rang sangs rgyas/_/sangs rgyas rnams kyi nyan thos kyang /_/sku lus 'di ni spong mdzad na/_/skye bo phal pa smos ci dgos/_/gang du gnas kyang 'chi bas mi tshugs pa'i/_/sa phyogs de ni yod pa ma yin te/_/bar snang la med rgya mtsho'i nang na med/_/ri bo rnams
[\[3a\]]
[\[3a.1\]]kyi gseb tu zhugs na'ang min/_/byung dang 'byung bar 'gyur ba ji snyed pa/_/kun gyis lus 'di btang nas 'gro ba dang /_/de kun 'jig par mkhas pas rtogs gyis te/_/chos la gnas kyis tshangs par spyad pa spyod/_/rga ba mthong zhing nad kyi sdug bsngal dang /_/
[\[3a.2\]]sems dang bral ba'i shi ba mthong nas ni/_/ston pas btson ra 'dra ba'i khyim spangs kyi/_/'jig rten phal pas 'dod spong nus re skan/_/rgyal po'i shing rta shin tu bkra ba'ang 'jig_/de bzhin lus kyang nye bar rga bar 'gyur/_/dam pa rnams kyi chos 'di dam pa ste/_/mi mchog
[\[3a.3\]]gzhan rtogs byed cing rga mi 'gyur/_/rga ba khyod ni blun zhing ngan/_/khyod ni mi rigs byed pa ste/_/yid du 'ong ba'i gzugs 'di yang /_/khyod kyis mngon par bcom par 'gyur/_/gang zhig lo ni brgyar 'tsho ba/_/de yang 'chi bdag nyid kyis khrid/_/'di dag dga' bar
[\[3a.4\]]'gyur ba'am/_/yang na na ba'am 'chi bas 'joms/_/rtag tu ldog pa med par 'gro 'gyur zhing /_/nyin dang mtshan du rab tu 'jig pa dang /_/skye dang 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa dang ldan pa/_/chu tshan nang du gdungs pa'i nya dang 'dra/_/tshe 'di nyin dang mtshan mo dang /_/'gro ba dang
[\[3a.5\]]ni 'dug pa na/_/chu klung chen po'i rgyun bzhin du/_/phyir mi ldog par 'gro bar 'gyur/_/chu chung nang gi nya lta bur/_/gang zhig nyin mtshan 'da' ba yis/_/tshe 'di shin tu thung 'gyur na/_/de la dga' bar byar mi yod/_/gson mtha' 'chi ba yin pa'i phyir/_/lus 'di yongs su
[\[3a.6\]]rga ba dang /_/nad kyi tshang 'di myur 'jig cing /_/rnag gi tshogs kyang 'jig par 'gyur/_/kye ma lus 'di mi thogs par/_/stong zhing rnam shes dang bral na/_/dur khrod bor ba'i mgal dum ltar/_/sa yi steng du 'gyel bar 'gyur/_/rgyun du nad kyis mngon gdungs shing /_/
[\[3a.7\]]rtag tu mi gtsang 'dzag pa dang /_/rga dang 'chi bas tsher 'grib pa'i/_/lus 'di dor ba cir mi rung /_/myur du 'jig cing na ba dang /_/rnag dang ldan pa'i lus 'di yis/_/grub dang bde ba bla med pa/_/zhi mchog don du gnyer bar gyis/_/dgun ka dang ni dpyid ka dang /_/dbyar
[\[3b\]]
[\[3b.1\]]ka 'di dag bya'o zhes/_/byis pa rnam par sems byed pas/_/bar chad mthong bar ma gyur to/_/bu dang nor phyugs 'byor pa la/_/mi yi yid ni rnam chags pa/_/'chi bdag gis ni blangs nas 'gro/_/nyal grong chu bos bdas pa bzhin/_/'chi ba'i dus la bab pa na/_/bu
[\[3b.2\]]rnams skyabs su mi 'gyur zhing /_/pha yang ma yin gnyen 'dun min/_/khyod la skyabs su 'gyur ba med/_/'di ni bya ba byas zin don 'di bya/_/de dag byas nas bdag gis 'di bya zhes/_/de ltar mi 'di yongs su shom pa na/_/rga dang nad bcas 'chi bas mngon du bcom/_/
[\[3b.3\]]de ltar rtag tu ting 'dzin la dga' mnyam par zhog_/brtson pa bskyed la skye dang rga ba'i mtha' ma ltos/_/bdud rnams sde dang bcas pa mngon par zil gnon la/_/dge slong dag go skye shi'i pha rol 'gro bar gyis/_/mi rtag pa'i tshoms te dang po'o//_//kun rtog
[\[3b.4\]]las ni 'dod skyes pas/_/'dod pa'i rtsa bar shes gyis la/_/khyod ni kun rtog ma byed dang /_/des na khyod la 'byung mi 'gyur/_/'dod pa rnams las mya ngan skye/_/'dod pa rnams las 'jigs pa 'byung /_/'dod pa dag ni rnam spangs na/_/mya ngan med cing 'jigs pa
[\[3b.5\]]med/_/dga' ba rnams las mya ngan skye/_/dga' ba rnams las 'jigs pa 'byung /_/dga' ba dag ni rnam spangs na/_/mya ngan med cing 'jigs pa med/_/'dod dga'i rnam smin sdug bsngal de/_/dang po mngar la 'bras bu tsha/_/me sgron lag nas ma bor ba/_/mjug tu
[\[3b.6\]]byis pa sreg byed bzhin/_/nor bu'i rna cha bu dang bu mo la/_/yongs su chags sems gang yin la ltos na/_/lcags shing gres ma las byas ching ma gang /_/de dag dam po min zhes 'phags pas gsungs/_/'dod pa'i ching ma gang yin de lhod kyang /_/rab tu dgrol bar
[\[3b.7\]]dka' zhes 'phags pas gsungs/_/brtan rnams 'dod pa'i bde la mi lta bar/_/de dag gtubs nas myur du 'gro bar byed/_/'jig rten sna tshogs gang de 'dod min gyi/_/skyes bu'i kun rtog gang yin 'dod pa yin/_/'jig rten sna tshogs de bzhin gnas kyang
[\[4a\]]
[\[4a.1\]]ni/_/'on kyang brtan rnams 'di la 'dun pa 'dul/_/mi rnams la ni rtag pa'i 'dod pa med/_/'dod can gang la chags de mi rtag pas/_/yang srid med phyir sems kyis rab spongs la/_/'chi ba'i gnas mi 'gyur bar byos zhes gsungs/_/
[\[4a.2\]]'dun pa skyes shing zad par mi byed dam/_/sems la skyon med pa dang dran pa dang /_/'dod pa rnams la so sor ma chags gang /_/de ni gong du 'pho ba yin zhes gsungs/_/mgar ba yis ni dngul bzhin du/_/blo gros ldan pas rim pa bzhin/_/skad cig skad cig cung zad tsam/_/
[\[4a.3\]]rang gi dri ma bsal bar bya/_/lham mkhan gyis ni ko ba dang /_/yongs su sbyangs nas lham byed ltar/_/'dod pa gang dang gang spangs pa/_/de de bde ba phun sum ldan/_/gal te bde ba kun 'dod na/_/'dod pa thams cad yongs su spongs/_/'dod pa thams cad yongs
[\[4a.4\]]spangs pas/_/mchog tu bde ba thob par 'gyur/_/ji srid 'dod pa'i rjes 'brang ba/_/de srid bar du ngoms mi 'gyur/_/de las gang dag shes rab kyis/_/ldog byed de dag tshim pa thob/_/'dod pas ngoms par mi 'gyur bas/_/shes rab kyis ni ngoms pa bskyed/_/
[\[4a.5\]]shes rab kyis ni ngoms pa'i mi/_/srid pa'i dbang du mi 'gyur ro/_/'dod la chags pa'i mi gang yin/_/de dag kye ma chos min dga'/_/cung zad gson por 'dug pa na/_/bar chad mthong bar mi 'gyur ro/_/blo ngan longs spyod kyis bcom pa/_/pha rol tshol bar mi
[\[4a.6\]]byed cing /_/bsam brlag 'dod la sred pa yis/_/bdag dang gzhan yang phung bar byed/_/kAr ShA pa Na'i char bab kyang /_/'dod pa rnams kyis ngoms mi 'gyur/_/'dod pa mnog chung nyes mang bar/_/mkhas pa rnams kyis khong du chud/_/lha yi 'dod pa rnams
[\[4a.7\]]la yang /_/lhag par dga' bar mi 'gyur gyi/_/rdzogs sangs rgyas dang nyan thos rnams/_/sred pa zad pas dgyes par 'gyur/_/gangs can dang ni mnyam pa yi/_/gser gyi ri bo yod gyur kyang /_/nor des gcig kyang mi tshim par/_/rtogs par gyis la legs par
[\[4b\]]
[\[4b.1\]]spyod/_/gang dag sdug bsngal de yi rgyur shes pa/_/de dag nam yang 'dod la dga' mi 'gyur/_/'jig rten dag na zug rngu'i rgyur shes nas/_/de dag gdul phyir bstan pa slob par byed/_/'dod pa'i tshoms te gnyis pa'o//_//lus can rnam par rtog pas
[\[4b.2\]]rab bcom nas/_/'dod chags mi bzad gtsang bar rjes lta bas/_/'dod chags phyir zhing rab tu 'phel 'gyur te/_/rang gi 'ching ba de yis dam por byed/_/gang dag rnam rtog nye bar zhi dga' zhing /_/mi sdug sgom pa rtag tu dran byed de/_/de yi sred pa rab tu
[\[4b.3\]]spangs pa yis/_/rang gi 'ching ba de dag 'drul bar byed/_/'dod pa mun nag dra bas g.yogs/_/sred pa'i dgab pas bkab pa dang /_/bag med 'ching bas bcings pa dag_/tshed mar chud pa'i nya dang 'dra/_/skyes bu bag med rab tu spyod byed pa/_/'khri shing
[\[4b.4\]]bzhin du sred pa 'phel 'gyur zhing /_/rga dang 'chi ba'i rjes su 'gro 'gyur te/_/ma drung nu zho 'dod pa'i be'u dang 'dra/_/mi dag dran par byed dang chags byed dang /_/yid bde ba la rtog par byed pa dag_/de yis yang dang yang du 'khor bar 'khyam/_/tshal nang 'bras bu 'dod
[\[4b.5\]]pa'i spre'u dang mtshungs/_/mi gang rtag tu bde bar 'dod byed pa/_/skye dang rga bar nye bar 'gro 'gyur zhing /_/skye dgu sred pa rnams kyis mdun du bdar/_/rgya nang ri bong yongs su rgyug pa bzhin/_/sred pa rnams kyis 'dud pa'i sems can dag_/srid dang srid min dag la sems
[\[4b.6\]]chags shing /_/kun sbyor ro la dga' ba'i byis pa rnams/_/yang dang yang du sdug bsngal thob par 'gyur/_/skye bo grub dang bde ba dang bral zhing /_/bdud kyi sbyor ba dag dang ldan pa de/_/rga dang 'chi ba'i rjes su 'gro 'gyur te/_/ma drung nu zho 'dod pa'i be'u dang 'dra/_/
[\[4b.7\]]'di na sred pa de 'dra spong byed pa/_/srid dang srid min dag la sred bral zhing /_/dge slong srid pa zil gyis gnon byed pa/_/lhag ma med par yongs su mya ngan 'da'/_/gang zhig 'jig rten spang dka' ba'i/_/sred pa'i bud med 'dis bkol ba/_/de yi mya ngan 'phel 'gyur te/_/
[\[5a\]]
[\[5a.1\]]rtswa la char pa bab pa bzhin/_/gang zhig 'jig rten spang dka' ba'i/_/sred pa'i bud med 'di spong ba/_/de yi mya ngan ldog 'gyur te/_/pad+ma las ni chu thigs bzhin/_/de phyir ji snyed 'dir lhags pa/_/khyed la smra yis khyed bde shog_/u shir
[\[5a.2\]]phyir ni rtswa bzhin du/_/sred pa rtsar bcas drungs nas phyung /_/skyes bu sred pa dang 'grogs na/_/yun rings dus su 'khyam 'gyur bas/_/sred pa drungs nas phyung shig dang /_/mya ngan med cing 'jigs pa med/_/yang dang yang du nyer len cing /_/yang dang yang du
[\[5a.3\]]mngal du 'jug_/gnas skabs 'gyur dang gzhan 'gyur bas/_/sems can 'ong dang 'gro bar byed/_/'dir ni spang dka'i sred pa de/_/spongs la sa bon chod cig dang /_/de la sred pa med 'gyur zhing /_/de ni yang du 'khor mi 'gyur/_/dal 'byor chud ni ma
[\[5a.4\]]gzan par/_/gang gis lha dang mi rnams su/_/don gnyer bcings nas 'jog byed pa/_/yul la sred pa de las rgol/_/sems can dmyal bar skyes na yang /_/dal 'byor thal bas 'gyod par 'ong /_/gang tshe srid mtsho'i rgyur 'gyur ba/_/yul la sred pa 'bras kyi
[\[5a.5\]]gzhi/_/'khri shing dra bas khebs byed pa/_/gdung bar byed pa ma btul na/_/sdug bsngal 'di ni yang dang yang /_/rnam pa kun du ldog mi 'gyur/_/dper na ljon shing rtsad nas ma bton na/_/bcad kyang phyir zhing skye ba kho nar zad/_/de bzhin sred pa'i phra rgyas ma bton
[\[5a.6\]]na/_/yang dang yang du sdug bsngal 'di mi ldog_/dper na bdag nyid kyis ni byas pa'i mtshon/_/de yis rkun po'i mthu yis bdag gsod ltar/_/de bzhin nang gi sems las byung ba yi/_/sred pas lus can nye bar gsod par byed/_/de ltar sred las sdug bsngal
[\[5a.7\]]dag_/'byung ba'i nyes dmigs shes gyis te/_/sred spongs nye bar len med dang /_/dran ldan dge slong kun du rgyus/_/sred pa'i tshoms te gsum pa'o//_//bag yod 'chi med gnas yin te/_/bag med pa ni 'chi ba'i gnas/_/bag yod 'chi bar mi 'gyur
[\[5b\]]
[\[5b.1\]]te/_/bag med pa ni rtag tu 'chi/_/de yi khyad par de rig pas/_/mkhas pa rnams ni bag dang ldan/_/bag yod pa la rab dga' ba/_/'phags pa'i spyod yul dga' ba yin/_/de la rgyun du sgom pa dang /_/rtag tu pha rol gnon brtan pa'i/_/brtan pas grub bde
[\[5b.2\]]bla med pa'i/_/mya ngan 'das la reg pa yin/_/gang tshe mkhas pas bag yod pas/_/bag med bcom pa de yi tshe/_/shes rab khang bzangs steng 'dzegs nas/_/mya ngan med pas gdung bcas dang /_/brtan rnams ri bo'i spo dag la/_/sa stengs byis pa rnams la
[\[5b.3\]]lta/_/brtson 'grus dang ni bag yod dang /_/yang dag sdom dang dul ba yis/_/mkhas pas gling du byas nas ni/_/chu bo chen po mngon du bzlog_/brtson 'grus ldan zhing dran dang ldan pa dang /_/spyod pa gtsang zhing brtags nas byed pa dang /_/yang dag sdom dang
[\[5b.4\]]chos kyis 'tsho ba dang /_/bag yod rnams kyi grags pa mngon par 'phel/_/lhag pa'i sems la bag bya ste/_/thub pa'i thub gzhi rnams la bslab/_/nyer zhi rtag tu dran ldan pa'i/_/skyob pa mya ngan med pa yin/_/dman pa'i chos la mi rten cing /_/bag med
[\[5b.5\]]pa la brtan mi bya/_/log par lta la 'dod med dang /_/'jig rten 'phel bar mi bya'o/_/'jig rten pa yi yang dag lta/_/chen po su la yod gyur pa/_/de ni tshe rabs stong du yang /_/ngan 'gror 'gro bar mi 'gyur ro/_/bag med pa la sbyor byed pa/_/skye bo byis pa bsam
[\[5b.6\]]brlag yin/_/tshong dpon nor rnams srung ba ltar/_/mkhas pas bag dang ldan par bya/_/bag med pa la mi sbyor zhing /_/'dod la dga' ba mi stsogs dang /_/rtag tu bag yod sems byed pa/_/zag pa zad pa thob par 'gyur/_/zag pa zad pa ma thob kyang /_/dus 'dir
[\[5b.7\]]bag med mi bya ste/_/ri dwags ma yis seng ge ltar/_/bag med pa dag bsad par 'gyur/_/bag med pha rol bud med sten byed pa'i/_/mi gang yin la gnas skabs 'di bzhi 'byung /_/bsod nams mi thob bde bar mi nyal dang /_/gsum pa smad 'gyur bzhi pa dmyal bar 'gyur/_/
[\[6a\]]
[\[6a.1\]]bsod nams ma thob sdig pa'i 'gro ba dang /_/'jigs dang bag tsha lhan cig bde ba chung /_/rgyal po'i chad pa chen pos gcod 'gyur zhing /_/lus zhig sems can dmyal ba rnams su 'tshed/_/gang zhig bdag bde lta 'dod pa/_/des ni gong ma bzhin du
[\[6a.2\]]bya/_/byis pa'i shing rta bzhin 'gyur bas/_/brtan pas brtson 'grus zhan mi bya/_/dper na byis pa'i shing rta dag_/lam chen bzang po bor nas su/_/lam ngan dag tu 'gro byed pas/_/mig chags sems khong chud pa ltar/_/de bzhin chos ni spangs nas kyang /_/
[\[6a.3\]]chos min rjes su 'jug byed pa'i/_/byis pa 'chi bdag dbang 'gro zhing /_/mig chags bzhin du bcom pa 'thob/_/gang zhig bya ba rnams spangs nas/_/mi bya ba dag byed pa dang /_/bag med pa yis rlom byed pa/_/de dag rnams kyi zag pa 'phel/_/gang gis zag pa
[\[6a.4\]]'phel 'gyur ba/_/de yi zag med rgyang ma na/_/gang zhig lus gtogs dran pa dag_/rtag tu legs par brtsams pa dang /_/bya ba ma yin mi byed cing /_/rgyun du bya ba byed pa dang /_/dran dang shes bzhin ldan pa de'i/_/zag pa rnams ni zad par 'gyur/_/gang gi zag pa
[\[6a.5\]]zad gyur pa/_/des ni zag med thob par 'gyur/_/ji tsam mang du smra byed pa/_/de dag dam chos 'dzin ma yin/_/gang dag 'di na thos nyung yang /_/lus kyis chos dag mngon sum byas/_/gang dag chos la bag byed pa/_/de dag dam chos 'dzin pa yin/_/gal te rigs
[\[6a.6\]]bcas mang du smras kyang ni/_/bag med mi dag de ltar byed mi 'gyur/_/dper na phyugs rdzis gzhan gyi phyugs bgrangs ltar/_/de dag dge sbyong skal ba thob ma yin/_/gal te rigs bcas nyung du smra byed kyang /_/chos kyi rjes su chos la spyod pa dang /_/'dod chags zhe sdang
[\[6a.7\]]gti mug spong byed pa/_/de dag dge sbyong skal ba thob pa yin/_/bag yod bsngags pa rjod byed cing /_/rtag tu bag med la smod pas/_/bag yod mchod sbyin brgya pa yang /_/lha rnams nang na gtso bor gyur/_/bya ba byas rung ma byas rung /_/mkhas pa bag yod bsngags pa
[\[6b\]]
[\[6b.1\]]brjod/_/bag dang bcas pa'i mkhas pa yis/_/don gnyis rab tu len par byed/_/tshe 'di'i don ni gang yin dang /_/phyi ma'i don ni gang yin pa/_/de dag brtan pas rtogs pas na/_/mkhas pa zhes ni brjod pa yin/_/dge slong bag yod la dga' zhing /_/bag med
[\[6b.2\]]pa la 'jigs lta bas/_/bdag nyid ngan 'gro las 'dren te/_/'dam rdzab las ni glang chen bzhin/_/dge slong bag yod la dga' zhing /_/bag med pa la 'jigs lta bas/_/sdig pa'i chos rnams sprul par byed/_/rlung gis ljon shing lo ma bzhin/_/dge slong bag
[\[6b.3\]]yod la dga' zhing /_/bag med pa la 'jigs lta bas/_/kun du sbyor ba phra sbom dag_/me yis bsregs pa bzhin du 'gro/_/dge slong bag yod la dga' zhing /_/bag med pa la 'jigs lta bas/_/kun du sbyor ba kun zad pa/_/rim gyis nyams su myong bar 'gyur/_/
[\[6b.4\]]dge slong bag yod la dga' zhing /_/bag med pa la 'jigs lta bas/_/'du byed nyer zhi zhi ba yi/_/zhi ba'i go 'phang so sor rtogs/_/dge slong bag yod la dga' zhing /_/bag med pa la 'jigs lta ba/_/mya ngan 'das dang nye ba'i phyir/_/yongs su nyams
[\[6b.5\]]'gyur mi srid do/_/brtson 'grus ldan zhing bag yod dang /_/chos spyod legs par spyod byed pa/_/'jig rten 'di dang pha rol du/_/chos spyad pa yis bde ba thob/_/zhi phyir bslab pa la brten dang /_/rtsol ba dang ni brtson 'grus skyed/_/mi dran pa dang bag med dang /_/
[\[6b.6\]]brtson 'grus chung dang kun sdom med/_/gnyid dang snyom dang g.yeng ba ste/_/'di dag bslab pa'i bar chad pas/_/khyed kyis yan lag de rtogs la/_/dran pa chud ni ma gzan cig_/dge slong tshul khrims bzang ba dang /_/bag yod pa la dga' ba yis/_/kun rtog
[\[6b.7\]]legs par mnyam zhog ste/_/rang gi sems ni rjes su srungs/_/brtsam par bya zhing dbyung bar bya/_/sangs rgyas bstan la 'jug par bya/_/'dam bu'i khyim la glang chen bzhin/_/'chi bdag sde ni gzhom par bya/_/gang zhig chos 'dul 'di nyid la/_/bag dang ldan par
[\[7a\]]
[\[7a.1\]]spyod byed pa/_/skye ba'i 'khor ba rab spangs nas/_/sdug bsngal tha mar byed par 'gyur/_/bag yod pa'i tshems te bzhi pa'o//_//sdug pa rnams las mya ngan skye/_/sdug pa rnams las 'jigs pa skye/_/sdug pa dag ni rnam spangs na/_/
[\[7a.2\]]mya ngan med cing 'jigs pa med/_/sdug gu ma las mya ngan skye/_/sdug las sdug bsngal sdug las 'jigs/_/sdug gu ma dag gzhan gyur na/_/yi mug 'gyur ba thob par byed/_/'jig rten sdug bsngal rnam pa du ma dang /_/mya ngan smre sngags 'don pa ji snyed pa/_/de dag
[\[7a.3\]]sdug pa dag las rten te 'byung /_/sdug pa spangs na de dag yod mi 'gyur/_/gang phyir 'jig rten 'ga' na'ang sdug med pa/_/gang yin de dag bde zhing mya ngan med/_/de bas gdung med rdul bral don gnyer bas/_/nam yang sdug par byed pa mi bya'o/_/sdug pa ma mthong sdug
[\[7a.4\]]bsngal la/_/mi sdug mthong na'ang de bzhin pas/_/nam yang sdug dang phrad mi bya/_/mi sdug dang yang phrad mi bya/_/sdug pa dang ni bye bral dang /_/mi sdug pa dang phrad pa yis/_/gang gis mi dag rgas byed pa'i/_/mya ngan mi bzad skye bar 'gyur/_/sdug pa shi bar gyur pa na/_/gnyen
[\[7a.5\]]'dun mdza' bshes mang po dag_/yun rings dus su mya ngan dang /_/sdug dang bral bas sdug bsngal 'gyur/_/gang la sdug dang sdug min med/_/de la mdud pa yod min pas/_/de ltas sdug nyid sdig can la/_/sdug par byed pa mi bya'o/_/sdug la bltas te don btang
[\[7a.6\]]nas/_/bde sbyor rnams la mi 'jug cing /_/bdag nyid mi bde'i sbyor ldan dag_/bde sbyor don ldan rnams la smon/_/gzugs sdug bde bas bsdams pa dag_/lha mi so so'i ris dag tu/_/sdig pa byed cing yongs nyams nas/_/rga dang 'chi ba'i dbang du 'gro/_/gang
[\[7a.7\]]zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/_/bag yod gzugs sdug spong byed pa/_/des ni spang dka' bdud zas dang /_/sdig pa'i rtsa ba'ang drungs nas phyung /_/legs min legs pa'i tshul dang ni/_/sdug min sdug pa'i tshul gyis dang /_/sdug bsngal bde ba'i tshul gyis su/_/bag
[\[7b\]]
[\[7b.1\]]med rnams ni mngon du 'joms/_/gal te bdag la dga' byed na/_/nyes par byed pas bde ba dag_/bde blag kho nar mi 'thob pas/_/'di ni sdig la gzhug mi bya/_/gal te bdag la dga' byed na/_/legs par byed pas bde ba dag_/bde blag kho nar thob 'gyur bas/_/
[\[7b.2\]]'di ni sdig la gzhug mi bya/_/dper na dgon pa'i grong khyer dag_/brtan pa'i 'obs kyis bskor ba dag_/gal te bdag la dga' byed na/_/'di ni bsrung bas legs par bsrung /_/gal te bdag la dga' byed na/_/thun gsum gang yang rung ba la/_/mkhas pas
[\[7b.3\]]mel tshe bya ba yis/_/'di ni sba bas legs par sba/_/dper na dgon pa'i grong khyer dag_/phyi nang srung bar byed pa ltar/_/dal 'byor chud ni mi zos pa/_/de ltar bdag ni bsrung bar bya/_/sems can dmyal bar skyes na yang /_/dal 'byor thal bas 'gyod par
[\[7b.4\]]'ong /_/phyogs rnams kun du sems kyis yongs brtags kyang /_/bdag las ches sdug 'ga' yang ma mthong ba/_/de ltar so sor gzhan la'ang rang sdug pas/_/de phyir bdag dgas gzhan la gnod mi bya/_/thams cad la yang srog ni sdug_/thams cad chad pas
[\[7b.5\]]'jigs pa na/_/rang gi nyams las dpag gyis te/_/brdeg par mi bya gsad mi bya/_/rgyang thag bcad par spyugs pa'i mi/_/ring nas nye zho med 'ongs nas/_/gnyen bshes mdza' bo lhags nas su/_/a la la zhes mngon par dga'/_/de bzhin bsod nams byas
[\[7b.6\]]pa'i mi/_/'jig rten 'di nas pha rol du/_/phyin tshe gnyen bzhin bsod nams dag_/'ongs nas mngon par dga' bar byed/_/de bas 'jig rten pha rol gyi/_/ched du bsod nams bsags par gyis/_/bsod nams 'jig rten pha rol du/_/lus can rnams kyi
[\[7b.7\]]gnas su 'gyur/_/gang zhig legs spyad spyod byed pa'i/_/dge la lha rnams stod par byed/_/'di na'ang smad par mi 'gyur la/_/mtho ris su yang dga' ba 'thob/_/chos gnas tshul khrims phun sum tshogs/_/ngo tsha shes shing bden par smra/_/rang gi bya ba byed
[\[8a\]]
[\[8a.1\]]pa la/_/skye bo gzhan rnams dga' bar byed/_/rang gi don ni byed pa la/_/'di ltar gzhan rnams dga' 'gyur zhing /_/mthong ba'i chos la bsngags pa dang /_/pha rol du yang bde 'gror 'gyur/_/gtam na gnang ba'i tshig smra dang /_/mi rigs spyod
[\[8a.2\]]las bzlog pa la/_/dam pa rnams ni dga' bar byed/_/dam pa ma yin dga' mi 'gyur/_/de bas mchog dang mchog min pa/_/shi 'phos bral bar gyur pa na/_/dam pa ma yin dmyal bar 'gro/_/dam pa mtho ris 'gro bar 'gyur/_/sdug pa'i tshoms te lnga ba'o//_//
[\[8a.3\]]bsngags par 'gyur dang nor 'thob dang /_/pha rol bde 'gror dga' 'gyur ba'i/_/bde ba gsum po don gnyer ba'i/_/mkhas pas tshul khrims bsrung bar bya/_/'phags dang mthong ba phun tshogs dang /_/'jig rten zhi ba rten 'gyur ba'i/_/gnas gzhan 'di dag mthong
[\[8a.4\]]ba yi/_/mkhas pas tshul khrims bsrung bar bya/_/lus la yongs su gdung med par/_/tshul khrims kyis ni bde ba 'thob/_/mtshan mo bde bar nyal ba dang /_/sad pa na yang dga' bar 'gyur/_/sbyin pa tshul khrims ldan pa dag_/mkhas pas byas pa'i bsod
[\[8a.5\]]nams kyis/_/'di dang pha rol dag tu yang /_/rtag tu bde ba 'thob par 'gyur/_/rgan pa'i bar la tshul khrims dge/_/dad la rab tu gnas na legs/_/mi yi rin chen shes rab ste/_/bsod nams chom pos dbrog par dka'/_/dge slong tshul khrims la gnas
[\[8a.6\]]shing /_/dbang po rnams kyang bsdams pa dang /_/zas kyi tshod ni rig pa dang /_/mi nyal ba la 'bad pa ste/_/de ltar gnas par brtson pa dang /_/nyin mtshan snyom las mi byed pa/_/mya ngan 'das dang nye ba'i phyir/_/yongs su nyams 'gyur mi srid do/_/mi ni tshul khrims
[\[8a.7\]]la gnas nas/_/sems dang shes rab sgom pa la/_/brtson zhing nges gnas dge slong gis/_/sdug bsngal zad pa thob par 'gyur/_/de phyir rtag tu tshul khrims dang /_/ting 'dzin rjes su bsrung ba dang /_/lhag mthong la ni bslab pa dang /_/shes bzhin so sor dran par
[\[8b\]]
[\[8b.1\]]bya/_/des ni kun sbyor zad byas nas/_/yid bral lhag ma med 'gyur te/_/lus zhig shes rab ldan pa yis/_/bgrang du med pa'i mya ngan 'das/_/gang zhig tshul khrims ting 'dzin dang /_/shes rab 'di gsum legs bsgoms te/_/shin tu dri med mthar phyin cing /_/
[\[8b.2\]]gdung med yang srid zad 'gyur dang /_/chags pa'i 'ching las rnam grol zhing /_/lus spangs shes rab ldan pa dang /_/bdud kyi yul las 'das pa dag_/nyi ma bzhin du lam mer 'bar/_/dge slong phyi dang nang nyid la/_/bag med rlom par byed pa yi/_/tshul
[\[8b.3\]]khrims ting 'dzin shes rab rnams/_/yongs su rdzogs par mi 'gyur ro/_/sprin gyis khebs las char 'bab cing /_/nam thang ba las char mi 'bab/_/de bas khebs pa sol cig dang /_/'di ltar char pa 'bab mi 'gyur/_/de ltar rtag tu mthong ba dang /_/dge
[\[8b.4\]]slong tshul khrims sdom pa yis/_/mya ngan 'das par 'gro ba'i lam/_/myur ba kho nar rnam par 'dag_/me tog dri ni rdzi phyogs min mi 'gro/_/rtsa ba rgya spos tsan+dan rnams kyang min/_/dam pa'i dri ni rdzi phyogs mi 'gro ste/_/phyogs rnams kun du mi mchog dri yis khyab/_/
[\[8b.5\]]rgya spos dang ni tsan+dan dang /_/ut+pa la dang ma li ka_/_spos kyi rigs ni 'di dag pas/_/tshul khrims dri bsung phul du phyin/_/rgya spos tsan+dan gang yin pa'i/_/dri bsung 'di ni chung ngu na/_/tshul khrims ldan pa'i dri bsung gang /_/des ni 'di dang mtho ris khyab/_/
[\[8b.6\]]de ltar bag yod gnas bya zhing /_/tshul khrims rnam par dag par bya/_/yang dag shes pas rnam grol na/_/bdud kyi lam ni rnyed mi 'gyur/_/'di ni bde bar 'gro lam ste/_/rnam par dag byed lam 'di la/_/rab tu zhugs te bsgoms nas kyang /_/bdud kyi 'ching
[\[8b.7\]]ba spang bar gyis/_/tshul khrims kyi tshoms te drug pa'o//_//lus kyis nyes par spyod spang zhing /_/lus kyis legs spyad spyad pa'i phyir/_/lus kyi nyes chen las bsrungs na/_/lus ni bsdam pa byas par 'gyur/_/ngag gis nyes par spyod spang zhing /_/
[\[9a\]]
[\[9a.1\]]ngag gis legs spyad spyad pa'i phyir/_/ngag gi nyes chen las bsrungs na/_/ngag ni bsdam pa byas par 'gyur/_/yid kyis nyes par spyod spang zhing /_/yid kyis legs spyad spyod pa'i phyir/_/yid kyi nyes chen las bsrungs na/_/yid ni bsdams
[\[9a.2\]]pa byas par 'gyur/_/lus kyis nyes par spyod spang zhing /_/ngag gis nyes par spyod pa spang /_/yid kyis nyes par spyod spang zhing /_/skyon gzhan ldan pa gang yin spang /_/lus kyis dge ba rnams bya zhing /_/ngag gis dge ba phal chen bya/_/yid kyis dge ba rnams bya zhing /_/
[\[9a.3\]]tshad med bzhi dang ldan par bya/_/lus kyis dge ba rnams bya zhing /_/ngag dang yid kyis byas na ni/_/'di dang pha rol dag tu yang /_/rtag tu bde ba thob par 'gyur/_/rtag tu lus ni bsdams pa'i phyir/_/thub pa 'tshe ba med pa yin/_/de ni 'chi med gnas 'gro zhing /_/
[\[9a.4\]]gang du song na'ang mya ngan med/_/rtag tu ngag ni bsdams pa'i phyir/_/thub pa 'tshe ba med pa yin/_/de ni 'chi med gnas 'gro zhing /_/gang du song na'ang mya ngan med/_/rtag tu yid ni bsdams pa'i phyir/_/thub pa 'tshe ba med pa yin/_/de ni 'chi med gnas
[\[9a.5\]]'gro zhing /_/gang du song na'ang mya ngan med/_/brtan pa rnams kyis lus bsdam zhing /_/brtan pa rnams kyis ngag kyang bsdam/_/brtan pa rnams kyis yid bsdam zhing /_/brtan pas kun du bsdams byas na/_/de dag 'chi med gnas 'gro zhing /_/gang du
[\[9a.6\]]song na'ang mya ngan med/_/lus kyi sdom pa legs pa ste/_/ngag gi sdom pa legs pa yin/_/yid kyi sdom pa'ang legs pa ste/_/thams cad du ni sdom pa legs/_/kun du bsdams pa'i dge slong ni/_/sdug bsngal kun las rnam par 'grol/_/ngag rnams bsrung zhing
[\[9a.7\]]yid rnams legs bsdams te/_/lus kyis mi dge ba dag spyad mi bya/_/las lam gsum po 'di dag rnam sbyangs na/_/drang srong gsungs pa'i lam ni thob par 'gyur/_/legs par spyad pa'i tshoms te bdun pa'o//_//gang dag byas bzhin ma byas zer ba
[\[9b\]]
[\[9b.1\]]dang /_/brdzun du smra ba dmyal bar 'gro bar 'gyur/_/mi de gnyis ka 'dra ba pha rol du/_/song nas dman pa'i chos dang ldan par 'gyur/_/skyes bu skyes pa'i kha nas ni/_/tshig ngan smra bar byed pa yi/_/tshig gi sta re skyes gyur nas/_/bdag nyid gcod par byed par 'gyur/_/
[\[9b.2\]]gang zhig smad 'os skye bo stod byed dang /_/bstod 'os skye bo rnam par smod byed pa/_/de ni kha yis 'thab krol kun stsogs shing /_/'thab krol can gang des ni bde mi 'thob/_/gang 'dir cho los rang nor 'pham byed pa/_/'thab krol de ni chung zad tsam du zad/_/gang zhig
[\[9b.3\]]bde bar gshegs la yid 'khrug pa/_/de 'dir 'thab krol shin tu chen po yin/_/ngag yid 'phags pas smad pa'i sdig bsten na/_/bye bar chu bur can dang stong phrag ni/_/bzhi bcu gcig tu chu bur rdol ba yi/_/sems can dmyal ba rnams su 'gro bar 'gyur/_/sdig
[\[9b.4\]]pa'i sems kyis ma nyes skyon brjod pa/_/bdag nyid gsad phyir dmyal ba spel bar zad/_/stobs ldan nyes pa dag ni bzod byed cing /_/de la sems kyang 'khrug par mi byed do/_/bsam brlag gang zhig sdig can gyi/_/lta la brten nas 'phags pa ni/_/dgra
[\[9b.5\]]bcom chos kyis 'tsho ba dang /_/bstan pa spong bar byed pa dag_/smyig ma 'bru chags lta bur ni/_/de ni rang gi 'bras bus gsod/_/tshig bzang kho na smra bya yi/_/sdig pa can dag smra mi bya/_/sdig can gdung byed smra ba bas/_/tshig bzang smra bar byed pa rung /_/
[\[9b.6\]]byis pa sdig can smra byed pa/_/smra ba'i tshe na 'ching 'gyur la/_/gal te smra na gzhan spong ba/_/de dag 'phags pa mi gsung ngo /_/dge slong dag ni bsdams pa dang /_/dal bus smra zhing rlom pa med/_/gang zhig chos ldan don ston pa/_/de ni snyan par smra ba yin/_/
[\[9b.7\]]legs par smra ba mchog ces 'phags pa gsungs/_/snyan smra mi snyan ma yin de gnyis pa/_/bden smra ba rdzun pa ma yin de gsum pa/_/chos smra phal pa ma yin bzhi pa de'o/_/tshig de rnams ni smra bya zhing /_/gang gis bdag kyang mi gdung la/_/pha rol la yang gnod med
[\[10a\]]
[\[10a.1\]]pa'i/_/tshig de legs par smra bar bya/_/gang gis mngon par dga' 'gyur zhing /_/gang gis sdig pa mi skyed dang /_/smras pas pha rol dga' 'gyur ba'i/_/snyan tshig kho na smra bar bya/_/bden pa'i tshig ni bdud rtsi ste/_/bden pa'i
[\[10a.2\]]tshig ni bla med yin/_/don dang chos la rab gnas pa/_/bden pa yin zhes dam pa gsungs/_/sdug bsngal thams cad spang ba'i phyir/_/sangs rgyas kyi sa ni gsungs tshig gang /_/bden pa mya ngan 'das 'gro ba'i/_/tshig de bla na med pa yin/_/tshig gi tshoms
[\[10a.3\]]te brgyad pa'o//_//chos gcig las ni rab 'das shing /_/'jig rten pha rol bcom pa yi/_/lus can brdzun du smra ba yis/_/sdig pa mi bya ci yang med/_/lcags sgong me lce 'bar 'dra ba/_/zos par gyur pa ches bla yi/_/tshul 'chal legs par mi
[\[10a.4\]]sdom pas/_/yul 'khor bsod snyoms bzar mi rung /_/khyod ni sdug bsngal gyis 'jigs shing /_/khyod la sdug bsngal mi sdug na/_/mngon sum dag gam lkog tu'ang rung /_/sdig pa can gyi las mi bya/_/gal te sdig pa'i las byas sam/_/byed kyang rung ste khyod
[\[10a.5\]]kyis ni/_/kog ces langs te bros byas kyang /_/sdug bsngal las ni thar mi 'gyur/_/gang du gnas na las kyis mi tshugs pa'i/_/sa phyogs de ni yod pa ma yin te/_/bar snang la med rgya mtsho'i nang na med/_/ri bo rnams kyi gseb tu zhugs kyang min/_/pha rol po
[\[10a.6\]]la brtags nas gang /_/sdig pa can gyi las mthong ba/_/de dag bdag gis mi bya ste/_/sdig byas las ni rjes su 'brang /_/las gang shin tu mi bzad dang /_/zol byed gzhal lugs 'chos pa dang /_/mi la 'tshe bar byed pa dang /_/gzhan la byed du 'jug pa yi/_/
[\[10a.7\]]las de mi yi rjes 'brang bas/_/de yis g.yang sar ltung bar byed/_/mi yis dge ba'am sdig pa yi/_/las ni gang dang gang byas pa'i/_/las rnams chud zar mi 'gyur te/_/de lta de ltar 'bras bur 'gyur/_/de yi tshogs pa ji srid par/_/de srid 'di ni gdung bar byed/_/
[\[10b\]]
[\[10b.1\]]de la gzhan dag gdung byed de/_/gdung byed de ni rtag par 'gyur/_/'di ni bdag rjes mi 'brang zhes/_/byis pas ma brtags byas pa yi/_/sdig pa'i las kyis 'gro ba dag_/pha rol du ni shes par 'gyur/_/gal te byis pas mi shes par/_/sdig pa'i las
[\[10b.2\]]ni byas pa dag_/nam zhig na ni de nyid kyis/_/rnam smin tsha ba so sor bsten/_/rang gi las kyis de 'og tu/_/me yis bsregs pa bzhin du gdungs/_/byis pa shes rab chung ngu dag_/bdag la dgra bzhin byed pa yis/_/gang zhig 'bras bu cher 'gyur ba'i/_/sdig can
[\[10b.3\]]las ni spyod par byed/_/gang zhig byas pas gdung 'gyur zhing /_/mchi mas gdong g.yogs ngu bzhin du/_/rnam smin so sor bsten pa yis/_/las de dag ni ma byas legs/_/gang zhig byas na mi gdung zhing /_/dga' zhing yid ni bde ba yis/_/rnam smin so sor bsten
[\[10b.4\]]pa yin/_/las de dag ni byas na legs/_/bdag nyid bde ba 'dod pa'i phyir/_/rgod bzhin sdig pa'i las byas pa'i/_/sdig pa'i las de'i rnam smin dag_/ngu bzhin nyams su myong bar 'gyur/_/nges par sdig las 'phral du ni/_/'o ma lta bur 'gyur mi byed/_/thal bas
[\[10b.5\]]g.yogs pa'i me lta bu/_/des ni byis pa sreg par byed/_/sdig las 'phral du nges par ni/_/mtshon bzhin gcod par mi byed kyang /_/sdig pa'i las kyis 'gro ba dag_/pha rol du ni mngon par 'gyur/_/gang du de dag rnam smin ni/_/tsha ba so sor bsten pa yi/_/sdig pa'i
[\[10b.6\]]las kyis 'gro ba dag_/pha rol du ni shes par 'gyur/_/lcags las g.ya' ni langs gyur pa/_/langs pa des ni de nyid za/_/de bzhin ma brtags byas pa yi/_/rang gi las kyis ngan 'gror 'gro/_/las kyi tshoms te dgu pa'o//_//dad dang ngo tsha tshul
[\[10b.7\]]khrims sbyin pa ste/_/chos 'di rnams ni skyes bu dam pas bsngags/_/'di yis lha yi 'jig rten 'gro 'gyur zhing /_/lam 'di nyid kyis lha yul 'gro zhes gsungs/_/'jungs rnams lha yi 'jig rten mi 'gro zhing /_/de yis byis pa sbyin pa'i bsngags mi brjod/_/brtan
[\[11a\]]
[\[11a.1\]]rnams sbyin la rjes su yi rang ba/_/des ni de dag gzhan du bde ba myong /_/'di na skyes bu'i nor mchog dad pa ste/_/'di na chos la legs spyod bde ba 'thob/_/bden pa kho na ro bro rnams kyi phul/_/shes rab kyis 'tsho 'tsho ba'i mchog ces gsungs/_/
[\[11a.2\]]mya ngan 'das par 'gro ba yi/_/dgra bcom chos la dad bskyed de/_/mkhas pas gus par mnyan na ni/_/de dang de yi shes rab 'thob/_/bag can gyis ni rgya mtsho dang /_/dad pas chu bo rnams las sgrol/_/brtson 'grus kyis ni sdug bsngal spong /_/shes rab kyis ni yang dag
[\[11a.3\]]'gyur/_/dge slong dad pa'i grogs ldan zhing /_/shes rab kyis ni gtams pa dang /_/mya ngan 'das la mngon dga' bas/_/'ching ba thams cad gcod par 'gyur/_/gang gis dad dang tshul khrims dang /_/shes rab nyid ni legs bsgoms shing /_/mkhas pas skyon rnams
[\[11a.4\]]spong ba de'i/_/legs pa'i ngang tshul can zhes brjod/_/dad dang tshul khrims phun sum tshogs/_/gtong ldan 'jungs pa rnam spangs pa/_/de ni gang dang gar song ba/_/de dang de ni mchod par 'gyur/_/mkhas gang 'tsho ba'i 'jig rten na/_/dad dang shes rab sten byed pa/_/de dag
[\[11a.5\]]de yi nor mchog ste/_/de yi nor gzhan phal par zad/_/'phags pa lta bar 'dod pa dang /_/dam chos nyan par dga' ba dang /_/ser sna'i dri ma rnam spangs pa/_/de ni dad pa can zhes bya/_/dad pa'i lam brgyags bskur bar bya/_/bsod nams chom pos dbrog mi nus/_/
[\[11a.6\]]chom rkun 'phrog par byed pa bzlog_/dge sbyong rnams kyis blangs na dga'/_/mkhas pas dge sbyong 'ongs pa la/_/mngon par dga' bar byed 'gyur zhing /_/skye bo rnams ni ci rigs par/_/dad pa ji bzhin sbyin byed cing /_/gzhan gyi zas dang skom de la/_/gang zhig yid ni mi
[\[11a.7\]]bde ba/_/des ni nyin dang mtshan rnams su/_/ting 'dzin thob par mi 'gyur ro/_/gang gis ta la'i mgo bcad ltar/_/de 'dra kun du gcod byed pa/_/des ni nyin dang mtshan rnams su/_/ting nge 'dzin dag thob par 'gyur/_/khron pa skam po ji lta bar/_/dad pa med pa bsten
[\[11b\]]
[\[11b.1\]]mi bya/_/ji ste de la yongs brkos kyang /_/'dam chu dri nga 'byung bar zad/_/chu mang rnam par dang ba dang /_/bsil bar gyur cing rnyog med pa'i/_/mtsho la chu 'dong ji lta bar/_/shes rab can gyis dad ldan bsten/_/chags sam ma chags kyang rung ste/_/de yis thub sku mi ngas
[\[11b.2\]]pas/_/ma dad pa dag spang bar bya/_/dad pa rnams ni nye bar bsten/_/dad pa'i tshoms te bcu pa'o/_/sdom la/_mi rtag 'dod dang sred pa dang /_/bag yod de bzhin dga' ba dang /_/tshul khrims legs spyod tshig dag dang /_/las dang dad pa de dag bcu//_//
[\[11b.3\]]bram zes 'dod pa rab spang zhing /_/brtson 'grus kyis ni rgyun chod cig_/'dod pa rab tu ma spangs par/_/thub pa gcig gis ma thob bo/_/kun du rgyu ba zhan pa dag_/nyon mongs phyir yang kun stsogs pas/_/brtson 'grus brtan po kho na yis/_/bya ba de nyid byed la
[\[11b.4\]]rag_/zhan pa'i las ni ji snyed dang /_/kun nas nyon mongs dka' thub dang /_/tshangs spyod yongs su ma dag de/_/don chen 'gyur snyam mi byed do/_/ji ltar mda' ni bzung nyes pas/_/lag pa chod par gyur pa ltar/_/dge sbyong bsrung ba bya nyes pas/_/dmyal bar nye bar khrid par
[\[11b.5\]]byed/_/ji ltar mda' ni bzung legs pas/_/lag pa chod par mi 'gyur ltar/_/dge sbyong bsrung ba bya legs na/_/mya ngan 'das par nye bar 'dren/_/dge sbyong rnam par ma shes dang /_/rgal bar dka' dang bzod dka' dang /_/gang dag zhan pa 'gyod 'gyur ba'i/_/sdug
[\[11b.6\]]bsngal mang po de dag 'byung /_/yang dang yang du 'gyod pa yi/_/kun rtog dbang du 'gro ba yi/_/sems ni bzlog par ma byas par/_/dge sbyong spyod pa ji ltar bya/_/nyes par rab byung nyes dga' ba/_/khyim 'dug nyes rtsom byed pa dag_/sdug bsngal mnyam med bsten pa dang /_/
[\[11b.7\]]yang srid sdug bsngal stsogs par zad/_/tshem bu ngur smrig gyon pa dang /_/phal cher yang dag mi sdom zhing /_/sdig pa'i chos can sdig la dga'/_/sdig can de dag ngan 'gror 'gro/_/sA la'i shing la 'khri shing ltar/_/gang zhig shin tu khrims 'chal te/_/ji ltar rang la
[\[12a\]]
[\[12a.1\]]dgra bzhin du/_/de ni de ltar byed par 'dod/_/mgo bo skya bor gyur bar du/_/da dung rgan rabs ma chud pa/_/de ni lang tsho gtugs pa ste/_/de ni rgan blun zhes bya'o/_/gang zhig dge dang sdig pa dag_/spangs shing tshangs par spyod pa dang /_/sde tshogs spangs

[\[12a.3\]]zhig sdig pa zhi gyur te/_/mkhas pas dge sbyong yin par shes/_/brtul zhugs med cing brdzun smra na/_/mgo bo bregs tsam dge sbyong min/_/gang dag sdig pa che phra dag_/kun la brtags nas byed pa dang /_/sdig pa zhi ba de dag ni/_/dge sbyong nyid ces brjod par bya/_/sdig pa

[\[12b.5\]]thug gdul bya dag bya dang /_/'khor ba'i skye shi zad par bya ba dang /_/khams rnams du ma so sor rtogs bya'i phyir/_/spyan dang ldan pas lam 'di rab tu bstan/_/ji ltar chu klung gang gA'i chu rgyun zhugs/_/rgya mtsho'i nang du 'bab par 'gyur ba ltar/_/de bzhin shes rab yangs
[\[12b.6\]]pas bstan pa'i lam/_/'di ni 'chi med thob par bya phyir 'jug_/gang zhig 'byung po kun la thugs brtse bas/_/sngon chad ma thos chos kyi 'khor lo bskor/_/skyob pa lha dang mi rnams 'dul mdzad pa/_/srid pa'i mthar phyin de la phyag 'tshal lo/_/rnam rtog dge ba

[\[13a.4\]]'dam bu smyig ma 'bras bus dang /_/chu shing 'bras bus bung ba ltar/_/pho bshal bkur stis phung bar 'gyur/_/ji srid blun po mchod byas pa/_/de srid rab tu brlag par 'gyur/_/byis pa'i dkar po'i cha 'grib cing /_/de yi spyi bo'ang nges par nyams/_/ngan pa rnyed pa

[\[16a\]]
[\[16a.1\]]'di na gang sngon bag med las/_/phyi nas bag dang ldan gyur te/_/sprin bral nyi ma zla ba ltar/_/'jig rten 'di na kun nas gsal/_/'di na gang sngon bag med las/_/phyi nas bag dang ldan gyur te/_/'jig rten 'di na sred pa las/_/dran pa

[\[16a.3\]]sred pa las/_/dran pas legs par 'da' bar 'gyur/_/gang zhig sdig pa'i las byas pa/_/dge bas 'gebs par byed pa de/_/sprin bral nyi ma zla ba ltar/_/'jig rten 'di na kun nas gsal/_/gang zhig sdig pa'i las byas pa/_/dge bas 'gebs par byed pa de/_/
[\[16a.4\]]'jig rten 'di na sred pa las/_/dran pas legs par 'da' bar 'gyur/_/gang zhig gson la mi dga' ba/_/de ni shi na'ang mya ngan med/_/brtan pa go 'phang mthong ba de/_/mya ngan dbus na'ang gdung mi 'gyur/_/gang zhig gson la mi dga' ba/_/de ni shi na'ang
[\[16a.5\]]mya ngan med/_/brtan pa go 'phang mthong ba de/_/gnyen 'dun dbus na lam mer 'dug_/dge slong dkar po bsgom gyis la/_/nag po'i chos ni rnam par spongs/_/khyim nas khyim med song nas su/_/spyod yul dben pa gang yin pa/_/de la mngon par dga'
[\[16a.6\]]bslab cing /_/'dod pa ci yang med par spongs/_/rtag tu snying po dag pa dang /_/rtag tu gso sbyong dag pa dang /_/gtsang ma'i las ni dag pa de'i/_/brtul zhugs phun sum tshogs par 'gyur/_/zhing gi skyon ni rtswa yin ltar/_/skye dgu 'di la 'dod chags skyon/_/de bas
[\[16a.7\]]'dod chags bral rnams la/_/byin na 'bras bu chen por 'gyur/_/zhing gi skyon ni rtswa yin ltar/_/skye dgu 'di la zhe sdang skyon/_/de bas zhe sdang bral rnams la/_/byin na 'bras bu chen por 'gyur/_/zhing gi skyon ni rtswa yin ltar/_/skye dgu 'di la gti mug skyon/_/de
[\[16b\]]
[\[16b.1\]]bas gti mug bral rnams la/_/byin na 'bras bu chen por 'gyur/_/zhing gi skyon ni rtswa yin ltar/_/skye dgu 'di la nga rgyal skyon/_/de bas nga rgyal bral rnams la/_/byin na 'bras bu chen por 'gyur/_/zhing gi skyon ni rtswa yin ltar/_/skye dgu 'di la chags pa skyon/_/
[\[16b.2\]]de bas chags dang bral rnams la/_/byin na 'bras bu chen por 'gyur/_/zhing gi skyon ni rtswa yin ltar/_/skye dgu 'di la sred pa skyon/_/de bas sred dang bral rnams la/_/byin na 'bras bu chen por 'gyur/_/drug pa bdag po rgyal po ste/_/chags par gyur na chags
[\[16b.3\]]can yin/_/ma chags gyur na ma chags yin/_/chags pa byis pa zhes brjod do/_/'dod chags zhe sdang nga rgyal dang /_/'chab pa gang du gnas pa yi/_/grong khyer rus pa'i ra ba can/_/sha dang khrag gis zhal zhal byas/_/rgyu yis kun nas bslang ba las byung
[\[16b.4\]]sdug bsngal can/_/de ma mthong na der ni de dag 'ching 'gyur zhing /_/de dag rtogs na chu bo rnams ni rab tu spong /_/phyi rol pa la chags pa de dag spong ba med/_/sil bu'i tshoms te bcu drug pa'o//_//de dag khyim la mi dga' bar/_/dran dang ldan pa
[\[16b.5\]]'bad pa yis/_/ngang pas mtsho ngan spong ba ltar/_/de dag khyim spangs chu bo rgal/_/brtan pa 'jig rten nges byung nas/_/bdud kyi sde rnams rab bcom ste/_/nyi ma'i lam nas ngang pa ltar/_/rdzu 'phrul gyis ni mkha' la 'gro/_/tshangs par spyod pa ma spyad cing /_/
[\[16b.6\]]gzhon nur nor ni ma rnyed pa/_/mtsho ngan nya nyung ngogs dag na/_/chu skyar rgan sems bzhin du 'gyur/_/tshangs par spyod pa ma spyad cing /_/gzhon nur nor ni ma rnyed pa/_/sngon chad byas pa rjes dran zhing /_/lus bskums nas ni nyal bar 'gyur/_/sdig pa chung byas
[\[16b.7\]]bdag nyid kyi/_/phyi bzhin mi 'ong ma sems shig_/chu yi thigs pa lhung ba yis/_/bum chen gang ba ji bzhin du/_/chung zad chung zad bsags pa yi/_/sdig pas byis pa gang bar 'gyur/_/dge ba chung byas bdag nyid kyi/_/phyi bzhin mi 'ang ma sems shig_/
[\[17a\]]
[\[17a.1\]]chu yi thigs pa lhung ba yis/_/bum chen gang ba ji bzhin du/_/chung zad chung zad bsags pa yi/_/dge bas brtan pa gang bar 'gyur/_/gang zhig rags brtsigs mtsho ngan spangs/_/rgya mtsho'i chu bo rgal 'dod pa/_/skye bos gzings ni bcas
[\[17a.2\]]nas kyang /_/skye bo mkhas pa rgal bar byed/_/rgal nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das/_/bram ze skam sar gnas par mdzad/_/de la dge slong khrus byed cing /_/nyan thos rnams kyis gzings kyang bcas/_/ji ltar mtsho chen zab mo dag_/rab tu mnam dang rnyog med
[\[17a.3\]]ltar/_/de bzhin mkhas pa rab dang pas/_/'di ni chos ni nyan par byed/_/'di ltar kun na chu yod pas/_/su zhig tshol zhing rgyu byed de/_/khron pa'i chu lta ci zhig dgos/_/sred pa rtsa nas gcad par gyis/_/btso blag mkhan dag chus 'khru zhing /_/mda' mkhan mes ni
[\[17a.4\]]srong ba dang /_/shing mkhan shing la 'jog sbyong ltar/_/mkhas pas bdag nyid gdul bar bya/_/nam mkha' lta bur chags med cing /_/sgo them lta bur g.yo ba med/_/rnyog pa can gyi mtsho lta bur/_/mkhas pa 'khor ba la mi dga'/_/chu'i tshoms te bcu bdun
[\[17a.5\]]pa'o//_//lhar bcas gshin rje'i 'jig rten 'di/_/sa stengs las rgyal gang zhing lags/_/me tog lta bur rab 'dod pa'i/_/chos bzhi legs par ston mkhas gang /_/lhar bcas gshin rje'i 'jig rten 'di/_/sa stengs las rgyal slob pa yi/_/me
[\[17a.6\]]tog lta bur rab 'dod pa'i/_/chos bzhi legs par ston mkhas te/_/nags tshal las ni 'jigs skyes phyir/_/nags tshal gcad kyi shing ma yin/_/nags dang nags sbyor chod cig dang /_/dge sbyong mya ngan 'da' bar 'gyur/_/gal te nags sbyor ma bcad na/_/
[\[17a.7\]]phra rab kyis kyang mi rnams skye/_/ma drung nu zho 'dod be+e'u ltar/_/de yis yid ni rab tu 'ching /_/lag pas ston ka'i pad+ma ltar/_/bdag la dga' ba bcad nas su/_/rgyal gsungs mya ngan 'das pa'i phyir/_/zhi ba'i lam nyid bskyed par gyis/_/ji ltar me tog yid 'ong ba/_/
[\[17b\]]
[\[17b.1\]]kha dog bzang yang dri med ltar/_/de bzhin legs par gsungs pa'i tshig_/'bras bu med par ma byed cig_/ji ltar bung ba me tog gi_/kha dog dri la mi gnod par/_/khu ba gzhibs nas 'phur ba ltar/_/de bzhin thub pa grong du rgyu/_/gzhan gyi skyon la mi brtag cing /_/
[\[17b.2\]]gzhan gyis byas dang ma byas min/_/bdag nyid kyis ni rigs pa dang /_/mi rigs bya la brtag par bya/_/ji ltar phyag dar phung po dag_/mi gtsang chu ni med 'di las/_/pad+ma kha bye gtsang ba dang /_/dri zhim yid 'ong rab skyes ltar/_/de
[\[17b.3\]]bzhin so so skye bo dag_/ldongs gyur phyag dar phung 'di las/_/rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi nyan thos dag_/shes rab kyis ni gsal ba 'byung /_/ji ltar me tog phung po las/_/me tog phreng rgyud mang byed ltar/_/de bzhin mir ni skyes pa yis/_/dge ba phal chen rnams
[\[17b.4\]]kyang bya/_/ji ltar dbyar ka ba ku la'i/_/me tog rab tu rnam 'brul ltar/_/de bzhin dge slong 'dod chags dang /_/zhe sdang gti mug spang bar gyis/_/mi yi yid la rnam chags dang /_/me tog bzhin du rab bsags pa/_/'chi bdag gis ni blangs nas 'gro/_/
[\[17b.5\]]nyal grong chu bos bdas pa bzhin/_/mi yi yid la rnam chags dag_/me tog bzhin du rab bsags pa/_/'dod pa rnams kyis mi ngoms shing /_/'chi bdag gis ni dbang du byed/_/mi yi yid la rnam chags dag_/me tog bzhin du rab bsags pa/_/longs
[\[17b.6\]]spyod skye bar mi 'gyur zhing /_/'chi bdag gis ni dbang du byed/_/mi yi yid la rnam chags dag_/me tog bzhin du rab bsags pa/_/bya ba mthar ni ma phyin par/_/'chi bdag gis ni dbang du byed/_/lus 'di bum pa 'dra bar rtogs byas shing /_/de bzhin chos
[\[17b.7\]]rnams smig rgyu 'drar shes nas/_/bdud kyi me tog mchog ni 'dir gcod pa/_/'chi bdag rgyal pos bltar yang med par 'gro/_/'jig rten 'di dag bum pa 'drar rtogs shing /_/de bzhin chos rnams smig rgyu 'drar shes nas/_/bdud kyi me tog mchog ni 'dir gcod pa/_/
[\[18a\]]
[\[18a.1\]]'chi bdag rgyal pos bltar yang med par 'gro/_/lus 'di dbu ba 'dra bar rtogs byas shing /_/de bzhin chos rnams smig rgyu 'drar shes nas/_/bdud kyi me tog mchog ni 'dir gcod pa/_/'chi bdag rgyal pos bltar yang med par 'gro/_/
[\[18a.2\]]'jig rten 'di dag dbu ba 'drar rtogs shing /_/de bzhin chos rnams smig rgyu 'drar shes nas/_/bdud kyi me tog mchog ni 'dir gcod pa/_/'chi bdag rgyal pos bltar yang med par 'gro/_/srid pa u dum bA ra'i me tog ltar/_/snying po med par sems pa'i dge slong
[\[18a.3\]]gang /_/de ni pha rol min pa'i pha rol po/_/spong ste sbrul rgas lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/_/chu skyes rtsa ba'i me tog chu gnas lta'i/_/'dod chags ma lus gcod byed dge slong gang /_/de ni pha rol min pa'i pha rol po/_/spong ste sbrul rgas lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/_/chu skyes rtsa
[\[18a.4\]]ba'i me tog chu gnas lta'i/_/zhe sdang ma lus gcod byed dge slong gang /_/de ni pha rol min pa'i pha rol po/_/spong ste sbrul rgas lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/_/chu skyes rtsa ba'i me tog chu gnas lta'i/_/gti mug ma lus gcod byed dge slong gang /_/de ni pha rol min pa'i
[\[18a.5\]]pha rol po/_/spong ste sbrul rgas lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/_/chu skyes rtsa ba'i me tog chu gnas lta'i/_/nga rgyal ma lus gcod byed dge slong gang /_/de ni pha rol min pa'i pha rol po/_/spong ste sbrul rgas lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/_/chu skyes rtsa ba'i me tog chu gnas lta'i/_/chags
[\[18a.6\]]pa ma lus gcod byed dge slong gang /_/de ni pha rol min pa'i pha rol po/_/spong ste sbrul rgas lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/_/chu skyes rtsa ba'i me tog chu gnas lta'i/_/sred pa ma lus gcod byed dge slong gang /_/de ni pha rol min pa'i pha rol po/_/spong ste sbrul rgas lpags
[\[18a.7\]]rnying rje ba bzhin/_/me tog gi tshoms te bco brgyad pa'o//_//ji ltar rta bzangs lcag gis gzhus pa na/_/skrag cing shugs drag 'gro byed ji bzhin du/_/dad pa tshul khrims ting 'dzin ldan pa dang /_/chos rnams rnam par gtan la 'bebs ldan zhing /_/dbang
[\[18b\]]
[\[18b.1\]]po mnyam gzhag bzod ldan 'grogs bde ba/_/skyob pa de rnams srid pa ma lus spong /_/ji ltar rta bzangs lcag gis gzhus pa na/_/skrag cing shugs drag 'gro byed ji bzhin du/_/dad pa tshul khrims ting 'dzin ldan pa dang /_/chos rnams rnam par gtan la 'bebs ldan zhing /_/rig

[\[18b.3\]]yis bag med dang /_/mi nyal mang pos gnyid log dang /_/rta bzangs kyis ni rta rgod ltar/_/shin tu mkhas pas spangs nas 'gro/_/rta bzangs la ni lcag bzhin du/_/gang zhig ngo tsha shes sten cing /_/shes rab legs par mnyam gzhag pa/_/des ni sdig pa sel bar
[\[18b.4\]]byed/_/dul ba 'dun sar 'gro byed cing /_/dul ba rgyal po lhag par zhon/_/gang zhig tshig ngan bzod byed pa/_/dul ba mi yi nang na mchog_/glang po'i nang na glang chen dang /_/sin du'i cang shes rta dang ni/_/dre'u 'dul byed pa gang yin pa/_/de bas bdag nyid 'dul ba mchog_/
[\[18b.5\]]bdag nyid legs 'dul gang yin pa'i/_/mkhas des zhi ba thob 'gyur gyi/_/bzhon pa de dag rnams kyis ni/_/sa de mngon par 'thob mi srid/_/glang po'i nang na glang chen dang /_/sin du'i cang shes rta dang ni/_/dre'u 'dul byed pa gang yin pa/_/de bas bdag nyid 'dul ba
[\[18b.6\]]mchog_/bdag nyid legs 'dul dran ldan gang /_/des ni sdug bsngal mthar phyin gyi/_/bzhon pa de dag rnams kyis ni/_/sa de mngon par 'thob mi srid/_/glang po'i nang na glang chen dang /_/sin du'i cang shes rta dang ni/_/dre'u 'dul byed pa gang yin pa/_/de bas bdag nyid
[\[18b.7\]]'dul ba mchog_/bdag nyid legs 'dul dran ldan gang /_/des ni 'gro rnams spong 'gyur gyi/_/bzhon pa de dag rnams kyis ni/_/sa de mngon par 'thob mi srid/_/glang po'i nang na glang chen dang /_/sin du'i cang shes rta dang ni/_/dre'u 'dul byed pa gang yin pa/_/de bas
[\[19a\]]
[\[19a.1\]]bdag nyid 'dul ba mchog_/bdag nyid legs 'dul gang yin des/_/'ching ba bcad nas 'gro 'gyur gyi/_/bzhon pa de dag rnams kyis ni/_/sa de mngon par 'thob mi srid/_/'dul sbyong byed pas rta bzangs ltar/_/bdag nyid kho na gdul
[\[19a.2\]]bar bya/_/bdag nyid legs par 'dul ba yis/_/sdug bsngal rnams kyi pha mthar phyin/_/bdag nyid kho na bdag gi mgon/_/bdag nyid bdag gi skyabs yin pas/_/'dul sbyong byed pas rta bzangs ltar/_/de bas bdag nyid gdul bar bya/_/rta'i tshoms te bcu dgu
[\[19a.3\]]pa'o//_//khro ba spangs shing nga rgyal rnam spangs na/_/kun sbyor kun las shin tu 'da' 'gyur zhing /_/ming dang gzugs la chags pa med de dag_/ci yang med pas chags pa'i rjes mi ltung /_/skyes ma thag tu khro ba spongs/_/skyes nas 'dod chags spang bar gyis/_/
[\[19a.4\]]brtan pas ma rig rab tu spang /_/bden pa mthong na bde bar 'gyur/_/khro ba spangs na bde bar nyal/_/khro ba spangs na gdung mi 'gyur/_/dge slong khro ba bde 'joms pa'i/_/dug gi rtsa ba chom shig dang /_/'phags pa rnams kyis bsngags 'gyur zhing /_/de bcom pa yis mya ngan
[\[19a.5\]]med/_/gang khros bdag gis legs byas kyi/_/ma legs min zhes rab smra ba/_/de ni khro ba zhi 'og tu/_/me yis bsregs bzhin gdung bar 'gyur/_/ngo tsha med cing khrel med pa/_/khro ba can la brtul zhugs med/_/khro bas mngon par zil gnon pa/_/de la su yang rten
[\[19a.6\]]mi byed/_/gang zhig byis pa'i mthu stobs can/_/de yi stobs ni stobs med yin/_/byis pa chos dang bral ba la/_/bsgrub par bya ba yod re skan/_/gang zhig stobs dang ldan gyur yang /_/stobs chung rnams kyi bzod byed pa/_/de ni bzod pa'i mchog ces gsungs/_/nyam
[\[19a.7\]]chung ba lta rtag tu sgur/_/gang zhig gzhan gyi dpon gyur kyang /_/stobs chung rnams kyi bzod byed pa/_/de ni bzod pa'i mchog ces gsungs/_/nyam chung ba lta rtag tu sgur/_/gzhan gyis lhag par brgyad bkag kyang /_/stobs ldan gang zhig bzod byed pa/_/de ni
[\[19b\]]
[\[19b.1\]]bzod pa'i mchog ces gsungs/_/nyam chung ba lta rtag tu sgur/_/gzhan gyis lhag par smad byas kyang /_/stobs ldan gang zhig bzod byed pa/_/de ni bzod pa'i mchog ces gsungs/_/nyam chung ba lta rtag tu sgur/_/gang zhig pha rol khros rig nas/_/bdag nyid nye bar zhi byed
[\[19b.2\]]pa/_/de ni bdag dang gzhan dag gi_/'jigs chen dag las skyob pa yin/_/gang zhig pha rol khros rig nas/_/bdag nyid nye bar zhi byed pa/_/de ni bdag dang gzhan dag gi/_/gnyi ga'i don ni spyod pa yin/_/bdag nyid dang ni gzhan dag dang /_/gnyi ga'i don ni spyod de la/_/
[\[19b.3\]]skye bo chos la mi mkhas rnams/_/byis pa yin zhes sems kyang sla/_/gtso bo'i tshig ni 'jigs phyir bzod byed dang /_/thab zla'i tshig ni 'thab gcugs rgyu bzod pas/_/gang zhig dman pa'i tshig la bzod byed de/_/bzod pa'i mchog ces dam pas rab tu gsungs/_/byis
[\[19b.4\]]pa khros nas tshig rtsub dag_/smras na rgyal bar 'gyur snyam sems/_/gang zhig tshig dag bzod byed pa/_/de ni rtag tu rgyal ba yin/_/bden par smra bya khro mi bya/_/slong la chung yang sbyin par bya/_/rnam pa 'di gsum gnas kyis ni/_/lha yi gnas su 'gro bar 'gyur/_/khro ba'i
[\[19b.5\]]zil gyis non pa'i mis/_/rang gi don kyang mi rtogs pas/_/'khor gyi nang du bag rkyong la/_/khro ba med pa'i tshig smros shig_/gang zhig khros la slar khro ba/_/de ni sdig pa can 'gyur bas/_/khros la slar ni ma khro dang /_/thub par dka' ba'i g.yul las rgyal/_/khro ba
[\[19b.6\]]med pas khro ba thub/_/legs pas legs pa ma yin thub/_/sbyin pa yis ni 'jungs pa thub/_/bden pas bden pa ma yin thub/_/dul zhing rigs pas 'tsho ba dang /_/khro ba med pa ga la khro/_/yang dag shes pas rnam grol ba'i/_/mkhas pa rnams la khro ba med/_/
[\[19b.7\]]khro ba med la 'tshe med la/_/'phags pa'i skye bos rtag bsten kyang /_/skye bo sdig can khro ba dag_/ri bo bzhin du sgur bar byed/_/gang zhig khro ba byung ba dang /_/shing rta 'khyams las 'dzin byed de/_/'dul sbyong mkhan du ngas gsungs kyi/_/zhags 'degs skye
[\[20a\]]
[\[20a.1\]]bo phal ba yin/_/khro ba'i tshoms te nyi shu pa'o/_/sdom la/_dge sbyong lam dang bkur sti dang /_/'khu dang lnga pa dran pa ste/_/sil bu chu dang me tog dang /_/rta dang khro ba bcu pa'o//_//'jig rten 'di na kun rig kun zil gnon/_/
[\[20a.2\]]'di na chos rnams kun gyis ma gos shing /_/kun spangs sred zad rab tu rnam grol ba/_/nyid kyis mngon mkhyen pa la su yis bstan/_/de bzhin gshegs pa lha mi'i ston pa ste/_/stobs rnams kun ldan thams cad mkhyen pa nga /_/byang chub brnyes nas nyid kyis rab ston
[\[20a.3\]]pa/_/mtshungs med mnyam med nga la su yis bstan/_/nga ni 'jig rten dgra bcom ste/_/'jig rten dag na bla med nga /_/lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten na/_/bdud rnams zil gnon rgyal ba nga /_/nga dang 'dra ba med pas na/_/nga la slob dpon su yang med/_/'jig rten
[\[20a.4\]]'di na gcig pu yis/_/rdzogs pa'i byang chub bla med brnyes/_/gang zhig zag pa zad brnyes pa/_/rgyal ba nga 'drar shes par gyis/_/sdig pa'i chos las nga rgyal bas/_/de bas nyi 'gro nga rgyal ba/_/'jig rten yul sred rgal ba yi/_/kun mkhyen sangs rgyas mya ngan
[\[20a.5\]]'das/_/'jig rten pa la ma bstan par/_/kun nas 'byung ba mi shes pas/_/bA rA Na sIr song nas su/_/ngas ni chos kyi rnga brdung zhing /_/'jig rten sus kyang ma bskor ba'i/_/chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar byas/_/dpa' bo de bzhin gshegs pa rnams/_/'di na
[\[20a.6\]]chos kyis 'dul bar mdzad/_/de dag chos kyis btul ba la/_/mkhas pa su yang smod mi byed/_/brtan gang ting 'dzin la zhugs shing /_/nges 'byung zhi la dga' ba dang /_/sku yi tha ma 'dzin pa yi/_/rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas grags ldan pa/_/shes rab myur
[\[20a.7\]]ba de dag la/_/lha dang mi rnams dga' bar byed/_/gang dag 'das pa'i sangs rgyas dang /_/gang dag ma byon sangs rgyas dang /_/gang dag da ltar rdzogs sangs rgyas/_/mang po'i mya ngan sel mdzad pa/_/bzhugs par gyur cing bzhugs pa dang /_/de bzhin bzhugs
[\[20b\]]
[\[20b.1\]]par 'gyur kun gyis/_/dam chos bla mar mdzad pa 'di/_/rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi chos nyid yin/_/de bas 'di na bdag dga' zhing /_/bdag nyid chen po [(]mdon [,]mngon [)]'dod pas/_/sangs rgyas bstan pa dran byas te/_/dam pa'i chos la bla mar bya/_/mi gang sangs
[\[20b.2\]]rgyas bstan pa la/_/dad pa ma bskyed byis pa de/_/rgud pa'i gnas su 'gro 'gyur te/_/srin mo rnams kyis tshong pa bzhin/_/mi gang sangs rgyas bstan pa la/_/dad pa bskyed pa shes rab can/_/de ni bde bar pha rol 'gro/_/sprin shugs ldan pas tshong pa bzhin/_/
[\[20b.3\]]de bzhin gshegs pa mnyam med mtshungs pa med/_/bde bar rnam rtog de bzhin rab dben pa'i/_/rnam rtog gnyis po spyod pa'i sangs rgyas rnams/_/mun bsal pha rol gshegs shing grags dang ldan/_/des ni brnyes bya brnyes shing yid dbang gyur/_/kun grol
[\[20b.4\]]zag zad rab tu rnam par grol/_/rnam grol thugs ldan tha ba zag med rnams/_/lus can 'jig rten rnams la phan phyir gzigs/_/'ga' zhig ri bo'i spo la 'dug nas su/_/'gro ba rnams la kun du lta ba ltar/_/de bzhin blo bzang mya ngan bral ba dag_/chos las byung ba'i
[\[20b.5\]]khang bzangs steng gshegs nas/_/skye bo skye rgas zil gnon mya ngan gyis/_/gdungs pa rnams la kun du spyan gzigs nas/_/'chi ba med pa'i sgo mo 'byed mdzad kyis/_/gang dag nyan 'dod the tsom bsal bar gyis/_/de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshoms te nyi shu gcig pa'o//_//
[\[20b.6\]]legs par thos dang legs spyod dang /_/khyim nas legs par byung ba dang /_/spong bar byed pas rab bskor cing /_/dge sbyong gi ni rjes mthun legs/_/byis pa mi mkhas pa dag ni/_/'chi ba med pa lta bur spyod/_/mkhas pa dam pa'i chos dag la/_/mtshan mo'i nad pa bzhin

[\[21a.1\]]bar du shes mi 'gyur/_/mig ldan mar me yod pa yis/_/gzugs rnams mthong ba ji lta bar/_/de bzhin dge dang sdig pa'i chos/_/thos pas rnam par shes par 'gyur/_/thos pas chos rnams rnam par shes/_/thos pas sdig las ldog par

[\[21b.1\]]legs gsungs thos pa snying por shes pa dang /_/ting nge 'dzin dag snying por shes gyur kyang /_/gang zhig bag med rlang por byed pa de'i/_/thos dang shes pa don chen mi 'gyur ro/_/gang zhig 'phags pas bstan pa'i chos dga' zhing /_/de bzhin lus dang ngag gis spyod byed pa/_/

[\[25b\]]
[\[25b.1\]]gyur/_/'du shes 'gags shing 'du byed zhi/_/rnam par shes pa nub gyur pa/_/'di 'dra 'di ni sdug bsngal mtha'/_/lta bas mthong bar gyur tsam dang /_/nyan pas thos par gyur pa tsam/_/rtogs par byed pas rtogs tsam dang /_/rnam par shes pas rnam shes tsam/_/'di
[\[25b.2\]]'dra 'di ni sdug bsngal mtha'/_/'di dang ma dang gdungs rab gdungs/_/'di 'dra 'di ni sdug bsngal mtha'/_/ma re ma dga' rab zhi dang /_/kun du 'dod chags bral gyur pa/_/'di 'dra 'di ni sdug bsngal mtha'/_/rten pa yod pas spyod par 'gyur ro/_/spyod pa yod
[\[25b.3\]]pas gzhol bar 'gyur ro/_/gzhol ba yod pas shin tu ma sbyangs par 'gyur ro/_/shin tu ma sbyangs pa yod pas 'gro ba dang 'ong bar 'gyur ro/_/'gro ba dang 'ong ba yod pas gzhan du shi 'pho len par 'gyur ro/_/gzhan du shi 'pho blangs pas 'di ltar gzhan du skye ba dang /_
[\[25b.4\]]rga ba dang /_na ba dang /_'chi ba dang /_mya ngan dang smre sngags 'don pa dang /_sdug bsngal ba dang /_yid mi bde ba dang /_'khrug pa 'byung zhing 'di ltar sdug bsngal gyi phung po chen po 'ba' zhig po 'di 'byung bar 'gyur ro/_/rten pa med pas spyod pa med par 'gyur ro/_/spyod
[\[25b.5\]]pa med pas gzhol bar mi 'gyur ro/_/gzhol bar ma gyur pas shin tu sbyangs par 'gyur ro/_/shin tu sbyangs pas 'gro ba dang 'ong bar mi 'gyur ro/_/'gro ba dang 'ong ba med pas gzhan du 'chi 'pho len pa med par 'gyur ro/_/gzhan du 'chi 'pho len pa med pas 'di ltar gzhan
[\[25b.6\]]du skye ba dang /_rga ba dang /_na ba dang /_'chi ba dang /_mya ngan dang /_smre sngags 'don pa dang /_sdug bsngal ba dang /_yid mi bde ba dang /_'khrug pa rnams 'gag par 'gyur zhing /_'di ltar sdug bsngal gyi phung po chen po 'ba' zhig po 'di 'gag par 'gyur ro/_/dge slong dag
[\[25b.7\]]ma skyes pa dang /_ma byung ba dang /_ma bcos pa dang /_'dus ma byas pa dang /_mi 'byung ba yod do/_/skye ba dang /_'byung ba dang /_bcos ma dang /_sems pas byas pa dang /_'dus byas dang /_rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba yod do/_/dge slong dag gal te ma skyes pa dang /_ma
[\[26a\]]
[\[26a.1\]]byung ba dang /_ma bcos pa dang /_'dus ma byas pa dang /_mi 'byung ba med du zin na/_skye ba dang /_'byung ba dang /_bcos ma dang /_'dus byas dang /_sems pas byas pa dang /_rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i nges par 'byung ba yod do zhes nga mi smra'o/_/dge slong
[\[26a.2\]]dag gang gi phyir 'di na ma skyes pa dang /_ma byung ba dang /_ma bcos pa dang /_'dus ma byas pa dang /_mi 'byung ba yod pa de'i phyir/_skye ba dang /_'byung ba dang /_bcos ma dang /_'dus byas dang /_sems pas byas pa dang /_rten cing 'brel par 'byung
[\[26a.3\]]ba'i nges par 'byung ba yod do zhes nga smra'o/_/skyes dang byung dang 'byung ba dang /_/bcos dang 'dus byas mi brtan zhing /_/rga dang 'chi dang rmongs pa yi/_/chos can rab tu 'jig 'gyur ba/_/zas kyi rgyud las byung ba yi/_/'jig 'gyur 'di la dga' mi bya/_/de yi nges par
[\[26a.4\]]'byung ba'i gzhi/_/rtog dang dpyod dang zhi ba dang /_/sdug bsngal chos rnams 'gags pa ste/_/'du byed nye bar zhi ba bde/_/dge slong dag de ni gang du yang gnas par mi 'gyur te/_sa la gnas par mi 'gyur/_chu la ma yin/_me la ma yin/_rlung la ma yin/_nam mkha'
[\[26a.5\]]mtha' yas skye mched la ma yin/_rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched la ma yin/_ci yang med pa'i skye mched la ma yin/_'du shes yod min med min skye mched la ma yin/_'jig rten 'di la ma yin/_'jig rten pha rol la ma yin/_nyi ma dang zla ba gnyis la gnas pa
[\[26a.6\]]ma yin te/_'di la dmigs pa med par ngas mngon par shes so/_/dge slong dag de la 'gro ba dang 'ong ba yod par nga mi smra ste/_gnas par ma yin no/_/'chi 'pho yod par nga mi smra ste/_skye bar ma yin/_'di lta bu 'di ni sdug bsngal gyi mtha' yin no/_/sa dang chu dang me
[\[26a.7\]]dang rlung /_/gang la'ang gnas pa ma yin pa/_/de la dkar pos gsal mi byed/_/de la mun pa'ang yod ma yin/_/de la zla bas snang mi byed/_/de la nyi mas mngon mi byed/_/thub pa bram ze gang yin pa/_/des ni rang gis rig pa yin/_/de ni gzugs dang gzugs med dang /_/
[\[26b\]]
[\[26b.1\]]sdug bsngal kun las rab tu grol/_/mthar phyin 'jigs pa med pa ste/_/rlom med 'gyod pa med pa yin/_/srid pa'i zug rngu gtubs pa ste/_/lus kyi tha mar gyur pa yin/_/'di ni mthar phyin rnams kyi mchog_/zhi ba'i go 'phang bla med pa/_/mtshan ma thams cad zad
[\[26b.2\]]pa ste/_/byang grol go 'phang 'chi med yin/_/mtshungs dang mi mtshungs 'byung ba yi/_/'du byed thub pas rab tu spangs/_/nang du mnyam bzhag dga' ba yis/_/sgo nga'i sbubs ni dral nas byung /_/sbyin kun chos kyi sbyin pas thub/_/dga' kun chos kyi dga' bas thub/_/
[\[26b.3\]]stobs kun bzod pa'i stobs kyis thub/_/bde kun sred pa zad pas thub/_/mya ngan las 'das pa'i tshoms te nyi shu rtsa drug pa'o//_//bdag las gzhan pa'i skyon dag ni/_/phub ma gtor ba ji bzhin du/_/gzhan gyi skyon mthong sla ba ste/_/rang gi skyon ni
[\[26b.4\]]mthong bar dka'/_/g.yo can cho lo 'jo ba ltar/_/rang gi de ni sbed pa dang /_/gzhan gyi skyon la lta byed cing /_/rtag tu 'phyas lang 'du shes can/_/de yis ring du chos mi mthong /_/g.yon phyogs chos ni rab tu 'phel/_/spyi rdol byed cing 'phrog rlom can/_/mi gtsang
[\[26b.5\]]las ldan khA lta bur/_/shin tu nyon mongs 'tsho ba can/_/ngo tsha med pa'i 'tsho ba sla/_/rtag tu gtsang ma tshol ba dang /_/thub chod mi byed 'dzem bag can/_/'tsho ba dag pa lta ba yi/_/ngo tsha shes pa'i 'tsho ba dka'/_/'jig rten mun par gyur 'di ste/_/de las
[\[26b.6\]]lhag mthong ldan pa nyung /_/rgya las shor ba'i bya lta bur/_/mtho ris la dga' shas tsam zhig_/byis pa lus kyis bcings gyur pa/_/mun pa'i 'khor gyis bskor ba yin/_/'jig rten nor la chags pa dag_/gzhan rdzas lta bur lta bar byed/_/bdag gis skye dgu
[\[26b.7\]]'di phyung zhing /_/gzhan gyis byas so snyam sems pa/_/bden pa min la bden lta bas/_/ci yang mthong bar mi 'gyur ro/_/de ni 'gas kyang mi mthong zhing /_/zug rngu mthong bar mi 'gyur ro/_/yul sred gang la skye bo chags pa yi/_/zug rngu de dag sngon chad mthong ba dang /_/
[\[27a\]]
[\[27a.1\]]de ni bdag gis byas snyam mi 'dzin cing /_/de ni gzhan gyis byas snyam mi 'dzin to/_/skye dgu 'di dag nga rgyal ldan/_/nga rgyal la chags nga rgyal bcings/_/rtsod par gyur pa'i lta ba can/_/'khor ba ldog par mi 'gyur ro/_/thob par gyur pa gang yin dang /_/
[\[27a.2\]]thob par bya ba gang yin pa/_/de dag gnyi ga rdul gyis yog_/rjes su nad pa slob par byed/_/gang zhig tshul khrims dang /_bslab pa dang /_brtul zhugs dang /_tshangs par spyod pa dang /_dka' thub dang /_nye bar gnas pa snying por byed pa de ni mtha' gcig go/_/gang zhig de
[\[27a.3\]]ltar lta zhing 'di skad ces 'dod pa ni gtsang ba'o/_/'dod pa ni bsod nyams can no/_/'dod pa ni longs spyod par bya ba'o/_/'dod pa ni skyon med pa yin no zhes smra zhing de dag lhag par 'dod pa rnams su lhung bar byed pa'i brtul zhugs len pa 'di yang mtha' gcig go/_/mtha'
[\[27a.4\]]gnyis po 'di dag ni dur khrod 'phel bar byed pa ste/_'di dag gis dur khrod 'phel bar byas so/_/mtha' gnyis po 'di dag ma mthong ba kha cig zhen par byed cing /_kha cig mngon par rgyug par byed la/_de dag lhag par zhen par byed cing lhag par rgyug par byed pa dag mig
[\[27a.5\]]dang ldan pas mthong ngo /_/mtha' gnyis po 'di dag mthong ba na zhen par mi byed rgyug par mi byed la/_de dag lhag par zhen par mi byed cing lhag par rgyug par mi byed pa yang mig dang ldan pas mthong ngo /_/de dag de ltar mi byed cing de dag de ltar mi sems na/_de dag gi lam du
[\[27a.6\]]mi gdags pa 'di lta ste 'di ni sdug bsngal gyi mtha' yin no/_/ji ltar chu bur mthong ba dang /_/ji ltar smig rgyu mthong ba ltar/_/de bzhin 'jig rten lta byed pa/_/'chi bdag rgyal pos mthong mi 'gyur/_/ji ltar chu bur mthong ba dang /_/ji ltar smig rgyu mthong ba ltar/_/de bzhin
[\[27a.7\]]lus la lta byed pa/_/'chi bdag rgyal pos mthong mi 'gyur/_/gang la byis pa mngon chags pa/_/de la mkhas pa chags mi 'gyur/_/rgyal po'i shing rta bkra ba ltar/_/lus 'di rtag tu blta bar gyis/_/gang la byis pa rmongs 'gyur ba/_/de la mkhas pa rmongs mi 'gyur/_/
[\[27b\]]
[\[27b.1\]]rgyal po'i shing rta bkra ba ltar/_/lus 'di rtag tu blta bar gyis/_/gang du byis pa nyams gyur pa/_/glang rgan rdzab tu chud pa bzhin/_/rgyal po'i shing rta bkra ba ltar/_/lus 'di rtag tu blta bar gyis/_/nad pa lta bur 'jig chos can/_/rma byung ba dang 'dra ba ste/_/gang yang
[\[27b.2\]]brtan par mi gnas pa/_/lus 'di rtag tu blta bar gyis/_/nad pa 'jig pa'i chos can ltar/_/gang yang brtan par mi gnas par/_/nor bu'i rna cha gdub 'khor gyis/_/brgyan pa'i lus la blta bar gyis/_/skra ni lan bu brgyad byas shing /_/mig sman gyis ni bskus pa'i
[\[27b.3\]]mig_/byis pa lhag par rmongs byed kyang /_/pha rol tshol bar mi byed do/_/mig sman gyis ni gsar bris shing /_/rnag can lus ni brgyan pa yis/_/byis pa lhag par rmongs byed kyang /_/pha rol tshol bar mi byed do/_/lus ni dri zhim gyis bskus nas/_/rkang pa btsag
[\[27b.4\]]gis byugs pa dag_/byis pa lhag par rmongs byed kyang /_/pha rol tshol bar mi byed do/_/gang zhig 'dod par kun sbyor 'brel chags shing /_/kun du sbyor ba'i skyon rnams ma mthong ba/_/'dod par 'brel la chags pa'i mi de yis/_/chu bo mtha' yas yangs pa rgal mi
[\[27b.5\]]'gyur/_/chags bral mchog dang tha ma thams cad dag_/'di la bdag dang bdag gir mi lta zhing /_/de ltar rnam grol sngon chad ma rgal ba'i/_/chu bo rab rgal yang srid med par 'gyur/_/gang zhig tshal spangs tshal med pa/_/nags tshal spangs nas nags su rgyug_/grol ba
[\[27b.6\]]'ching bar gcen pa yin/_/gang zag 'di la ltos shig tshur/_/shing rta mthun pa'i rtsibs ldan pa/_/yan lag yid 'ong gos dkar g.yogs/_/sdig med 'gro ba la ltos la/_/ching ma'i rgyun rnams bcad par gyis/_/'jigs pas skrag pa'i mi dag ni/_/phal cher ri dang
[\[27b.7\]]nags tshal dang /_/skyed mos tshal dang mchod gnas dang /_/ljon shing rnams la skyabs su 'gro/_/skyabs de gtso bo ma yin zhing /_/skyabs de mchog tu gyur pa min/_/de la skyabs su song ba yis/_/sdug bsngal kun las grol mi 'gyur/_/gang zhig sangs rgyas chos dang ni/_/
[\[28a\]]
[\[28a.1\]]dge 'dun la ni skyabs song zhing /_/sdug bsngal sdug bsngal kun 'byung dang /_/sdug bsngal yang dag 'das pa dang /_/bde ba mya ngan 'das 'gro ba'i/_/'phags lam yan lag brgyad pa ste/_/'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po dag_/gang tshe shes rab
[\[28a.2\]]kyis mthong ba/_/de ni skyabs kyi mchog yin zhing /_/de ni skyabs kyi dam pa yin/_/de la skyabs su song ba yis/_/sdug bsngal kun las grol bar 'gyur/_/mthong bas mthong zhing mthong bas ma mthong mthong /_/ma mthong mi mthong mthong bya mthong mi 'gyur/_/'dra
[\[28a.3\]]mthong lhag mthong tha dad dngos por brjod/_/nyin mtshan nam yang lhan cig mi gnas bzhin/_/'dra ba mthong bas mthong mi 'gyur/_/gal te mthong na 'dra mi mthong /_/mthong 'dis 'dra ba mi mthong ste/_/'dra mthong mi yis mthong ba med/_/mi yis ci ma mthong na
[\[28a.4\]]'dra ba mthong /_/ci zhig mthong na 'dra ba mthong mi 'gyur/_/ji ltar 'di na 'dra ba mthong ba dag_/gang zhig med na 'dra bar mthong dang bral/_/gang tshe 'di yis sdug bsngal ma mthong ba/_/de yi tshe na bdag tu mthong bar 'gyur/_/ji lta ji ltar sdug bsngal rtogs gyur pa/_/
[\[28a.5\]]des ni bdag 'di 'dra ba mthong mi 'gyur/_/gang gis so so'i skye bsgribs na/_/'du byed sdug bsngal ma mthong ba/_/de phyir 'di na 'dra mthong ste/_/de med 'dra ba mi mthong ngo /_/mthong ba'i tshoms te nyi shu rtsa bdun pa'o//_//sdig pa thams cad mi bya ste/_/dge ba phun
[\[28a.6\]]sum tshogs par bya/_/rang gi sems ni yongs su gdul/_/'di ni sangs rgyas bstan pa yin/_/sbyin pas bsod nams rab tu 'phel/_/legs bsdams dgra sogs mi 'gyur ro/_/dge dang ldan pas sdig pa spong /_/nyon mongs zad pas mya ngan 'da'/_/mkhas dang 'dre dang
[\[28a.7\]]byis pa'i skye bo dang /_/lhan cig spyod dang gcig pu gnas kyang rung /_/ngang pas chu la 'o ma 'thung ba ltar/_/mkhas pas sdig pa can rnams rab tu spang /_/'jig rten nyes dmigs mthong ba dang /_/'gog par 'gyur pa'i chos mthong bas/_/'phags pa sdig la dga' mi byed/_/
[\[28b\]]
[\[28b.1\]]sdig can dge la dga' mi 'gyur/_/legs par nyer zhi'i ro dang ni/_/rab tu dben pa'i ro shes pa/_/rims nad med cing sdig med la/_/chos la dga' ba'i ro dag 'thung /_/sems kyi zag pa med pa dang /_/sems ni 'ching bas ma bcom la/_/dge dang sdig pa rab spangs pa/_/
[\[28b.2\]]ngan 'gro rnams kyis 'jigs pa med/_/gnas min zlog dang legs smra dang /_/nyes dmigs ston par byed pa dang /_/mkhas pas tshar gcod smra byed pa/_/de lta'i skye dgu bsten par bya/_/de lta bu dag bsten byas na/_/sdig par mi 'gyur legs par 'gyur/_/nye bar zhi zhing
[\[28b.3\]]rab zhi la/_/dal bus smra zhing khengs med pa/_/sdig pa'i chos rnams sprug byed de/_/rlung gis ljon shing lo ma bzhin/_/gang zhig skyes bu dag cing nyon mongs med/_/rab tu sdang med mi la khro byed pa'i/_/byis pa de la sdig pa phyir 'gog ste/_/rdzi phyogs su ni rdul rnams gtor
[\[28b.4\]]ba bzhin/_/dge ba byed pas dge ba dang /_/sdig pa byed pas sdig pa ste/_/mi yis gang dang gang byas pa/_/de de rang gis mthong bar 'gyur/_/bdag gis sdig pa byas na ni/_/de bdag kho na kun nyon mongs/_/bdag gis sdig pa ma byas na/_/bdag nyid kho na rnam par dag_/
[\[28b.5\]]gzhan gyis gzhan spyod mi byed kyi/_/dag dang ma dag rang rang byed/_/bdag nyid kyis ni sdig pa dag_/byas shing nye bar bsags pa yis/_/bsam brlag mngon du 'joms par byed/_/rdo rjes nor bu 'bigs pa bzhin/_/mig ldan 'gro bar byed pa yis/_/nyam nga'i lam dag
[\[28b.6\]]ji lta bar/_/mkhas pas 'tsho ba'i 'jig rten 'dir/_/sdig pa dag ni yongs su spang /_/nor chen gyis ni grogs nyung dang /_/tshong pas 'jigs bcas lam dang ni/_/gson par 'dod pas dug lta bur/_/mkhas pas sdig can yongs su spang /_/gal te lag mthil rma med na/_/
[\[28b.7\]]lag pas dug ni bzung byas kyang /_/rma med dug ni mi 'jen ltar/_/ma byas pa la sdig pa med/_/bdag la mi phan bya ba dang /_/legs pa ma yin bya bar sla/_/gang dag phan zhing bder 'gyur ba/_/de ni mchog tu bya bar dka'/_/dam pas legs pa bya sla yi/_/dam pas
[\[29a\]]
[\[29a.1\]]sdig pa bya bar dka'/_/ngan pas sdig pa bya sla yi/_/'phags pas sdig pa bya bar dka'/_/ji srid sdig pa ma smin pa/_/de srid byis pa mngar bar sems/_/gang tshe sdig pa smin gyur pa/_/de tshe de ni tsha bar sems/_/ji srid sdig pa ma smin pa/_/de srid sdig pa
[\[29a.2\]]rung bar lta/_/gang tshe sdig pa smin gyur pa/_/de tshe sdig pa mthong bar 'gyur/_/ji srid bzang po ma smin pa/_/de srid bzang po sdig par mthong /_/gang tshe bzang po smin gyur pa/_/de tshe bzang por mthong bar 'gyur/_/sdig pa sdug bsngal sogs pas na/_/de la dga' bar mi
[\[29a.3\]]bya'o/_/brgya la sdig pa byas na yang /_/yang dang yang du de mi bya/_/bsod nams bde ba sogs pas na/_/de nyid la ni dga' bar bya/_/gal te bsod nams byas na yang /_/de ni yang dang yang du bya/_/sdig la yid ni mngon dga' ba/_/bsod nams dal bus byed 'gyur bas/_/
[\[29a.4\]]sdig pa las ni sems bzlog cing /_/bsod nams mngon par smyur te bya/_/sdig pa chung ngu byas pas kyang /_/'jig rten pha rol 'jig chen dang /_/phung khrol chen po byed 'gyur te/_/khong par song ba'i dug bzhin no/_/bsod nams chung ngu byas pas kyang /_/'jig rten pha
[\[29a.5\]]rol bde bar 'dren/_/don chen dag kyang byed 'gyur te/_/'bru rnams phun sum 'byor pa bzhin/_/gang zhig nyes med chad pas gcod/_/sngar ba min la rab sdang ba/_/gnas gzhan gang yang rung ba bcu/_/myur du thob pa kho nar 'gyur/_/tshor ba mi bzad pa dag gam/_/yang
[\[29a.6\]]na lus ni 'dral ba'am/_/gnod pa'i tshor ba tsha ba'ang rung /_/yang na sems 'khrugs thob par 'gyur/_/gnyen 'dun rnams dang bral ba'am/_/longs spyod zad par 'gyur ba'am/_/rgyal po'i gnod pa 'byung ba'am/_/mi snyan shin tu mi bzad dam/_/yang na khyim ni
[\[29a.7\]]me chen pos/_/nges par sreg par byed par 'gyur/_/shes rab 'chal ba lus zhig nas/_/bcu pa ngan 'gror 'gro bar 'gyur/_/sdig pa byas pas bag dbab mi bya ste/_/ring byas rgyang mar byas kyang bag mi dbab/_/dben par byas kyang bag dbab mi bya ste/_/de yi
[\[29b\]]
[\[29b.1\]]rnam smin yod pas bag mi dbab/_/bsod nams byas pas bag ni dbab bya ste/_/ring byas rgyang ring byas kyang bag dbab cing /_/dben par byas kyang bag ni dbab par bya/_/de yi rnam smin yod pas bag dbab po/_/bdag gis sdig pa byas pas mya ngan byed/_/ring dang rgyang
[\[29b.2\]]ring byas pas mya ngan byed/_/bdag gis dben par byas pas mya ngan byed/_/de yi rnam smin yod pas mya ngan byed/_/bdag nyid nag po'i las dang ldan mthong nas/_/'dir yang mya ngan gzhan du'ang mya ngan byed/_/sdig pa byas pas gnyi gar mya ngan byed/_/de ni mya ngan de rab
[\[29b.3\]]mya ngan byed/_/bdag gis bsod nams byas pas dga' bar 'gyur/_/ring dang rgyang ring byas pas dga' bar 'gyur/_/bdag gis dben par byas pas dga' bar 'gyur/_/de yi rnam smin yod pas dga' bar 'gyur/_/bdag nyid rnam dag las dang ldan mthong nas/_/'di
[\[29b.4\]]na dga' 'gyur gzhan du'ang dga' bar 'gyur/_/bsod nams byas pas gnyi gar dga' 'gyur zhing /_/de ni dga' 'gyur de rab dga' bar 'gyur/_/bdag gis sdig pa byas pas gdung 'gyur zhing /_/ring byas rgyang ring byas pas gdung bar 'gyur/_/bdag gis dben
[\[29b.5\]]par byas pas gdung 'gyur zhing /_/de yi rnam smin yod pas gdung bar 'gyur/_/bdag nyid nag po'i las dang ldan mthong nas/_/'di na gdung 'gyur pha rol gdung bar 'gyur/_/sdig pa byas pas gnyi gar gdung 'gyur zhing /_/de ni gdung 'gyur de rab gdung bar 'gyur/_/
[\[29b.6\]]bdag gis bsod nams byas pas dga' 'gyur zhing /_/ring byas rgyang ring byas pas dga' bar 'gyur/_/bdag gis dben par byas pas dga' 'gyur zhing /_/de yi rnam smin yod pas dga' bar 'gyur/_/bdag nyid dkar po'i las dang ldan mthong nas/_/'di na dga'
[\[29b.7\]]'gyur pha rol dga' bar 'gyur/_/bsod nams byas pas gnyi gar 'ga' 'gyur zhing /_/de ni dga' 'gyur de rab dga' bar 'gyur/_/sdig pa byas shing bsod nams ma byas la/_/chos dang gol zhing chos min thob pa'i mi/_/sdig pa'i las can 'chi bas 'jigs 'gyur
[\[30a\]]
[\[30a.1\]]te/_/chu chen nang du gru ngan zhig pa bzhin/_/bsod nams byas shing sdig pa ma byas la/_/dam pa rnams kyi sngon gyi chos spyod pas/_/da ni nams kyang 'chi bas 'jigs med de/_/brtan pa'i gru yis pha rol 'gro ba bzhin/_/sdig pa'i tshoms te nyi shu
[\[30a.2\]]rtsa brgyad pa'o//_//ji srid nyi ma ma shar ba/_/de srid srin bu me khyer snang /_/nyi ma shar bar gyur pa na/_/snang ba med cing sngon por 'gyur/_/ji srid de bzhin gshegs ma shar/_/de srid rtog ge pa rnams snang /_/'jig rten rdzogs sangs rgyas shar ba/_/rtog can
[\[30a.3\]]nyan thos bcas mi snang /_/gces min gces par blos 'dzin cing /_/gces la gces pa min rtog pa/_/log par kun rtog spyod yul can/_/des ni gces pa thob mi 'gyur/_/gces pa min la gces min dang /_/gces la gces par 'du shes pa/_/legs par
[\[30a.4\]]kun rtog spyod yul can/_/des ni gces pa 'thob par 'gyur/_/'di na lta dang nyan la mngon zhen pa'i/_/chings ma gsar dang gsar du 'phel ba dag_/'khor bar rgyug cing 'gro dang sdod 'gyur te/_/me nang lhung ba'i phye ma leb dang 'dra/_/'di la myong 'gyur gzhan la myong 'gyur
[\[30a.5\]]ba'am/_/'di na the tshom tha dad ji snyed pa/_/de dag tshangs par spyad spyod 'bad pa dang /_/sems par byed pas rab tu rnam par spong /_/gang zhig snyigs ma yod bzhin du/_/ngur smrig gos ni gyon byed pa/_/dul dang des pa med pa de/_/ngur smrig gyon pa'i 'os ma yin/_/gang

[\[30b\]]
[\[30b.1\]]legs par ma brtags bar du mi dag gi/_/mdog gzugs lan 'ga' mthong bas yid ma rton/_/ra gan kha bsgyur lta bur mi 'tsham zhing /_/lcags phyed gser gyis g.yogs pa ji lta bur/_/khong pa rab gdug phyi rol 'phags tshul gyis/_/'jig rten 'di na 'khor
[\[30b.2\]]dang bcas par rgyu/_/gang zhig rde 'gengs gnyid ni log pa dang /_/nyin dang mtshan du 'gre ldog nyal byed pa/_/rdzab nang phag chen lus rgyas ji lta bar/_/yang dang yang du smad pa'i mngal du 'jug_/mi ni rtag tu dran pa ldan pa dang /_/rtag tu kha zas kyi ni tshod shes pa/_/
[\[30b.3\]]de yi sdug bsngal chung bar 'gyur ba dang /_/dal bus 'ju bas tshe yang ring bar byed/_/gang zhig dbang po ma bsdams shing /_/zas kyi tshod ni mi shes la/_/dran pa nyams dang le lo can/_/gtsang bar lta zhing gnas byed pa/_/de ni 'dod chags rnams kyis bcom/_/rlung
[\[30b.4\]]gis mi brtan ljon shing bzhin/_/gang zhig dbang po legs bsdams shing /_/zas kyi tshod ni shes pa dang /_/so sor dran zhing brtson 'grus ldan/_/mi gtsang lta bas gnas byed pa/_/de ni 'dod chags kyis mi choms/_/rlung gis ri bo mi g.yos bzhin/_/dgon pa dga'
[\[30b.5\]]bar bya 'os pa/_/de la skye bo mi dga' yang /_/de la 'dod chags bral ba dga'/_/'dod pa tshol bar byed rnams min/_/dgon pa'am yang na grong dag gam/_/gshang ngam thang bu dag kyang rung /_/gang na 'phags pa bzhugs pa yi/_/sa de yid du 'ong ba yin/_/dam pa ring
[\[30b.6\]]nas snang gyur te/_/gangs can gyi ni ri bo bzhin/_/ngan pa nye yang mi snang ste/_/mun khrod mda' ni 'phangs pa bzhin/_/mkhas pa don sems byed pa yi/_/dam pa nyid dang 'grogs na ni/_/don chen 'gyur zhing zab mo yi/_/shes rab so sor rtogs par 'gyur/_/gzhu yis

[\[31a.1\]]pha ma dag ni bsad byas shing /_/rgyal po gtsang sbra can gnyis dang /_/yul 'khor 'khor dang bcas bcom na/_/mi ni dag par 'gyur zhes bya/_/gang dag kun du sogs med cing /_/gang dag kha zas yongs shes pa/_/stong dang mtshan ma med pa

[\[33a.1\]]min spyad na ni/_/'gro ba gang yang rung ba ngan 'gror 'gro/_/'di na sbrul nag rked nas bzung ba ltar/_/chos min spyod pa de dag rlag par 'gyur/_/chos dang chos min gnyi ga yi/_/rnam smin 'dra bar mi 'gyur te/_/chos ma yin pas dmyal bar

[\[33b.1\]]'thob bde bar ni/_/mthong ba'i chos la mya ngan 'da'/_/'khon dang 'jigs pa kun 'das shing /_/'jig rten yul gyi sred las rgal/_/chos thos pa dang mthong ba dang /_/dben par dga' ba bde ba ste/_/'jig rten srog chags 'byung po la/_/'tshe med yang

[\[33b.3\]]bde/_/sdig pa mi byed pa dag bde/_/'jig rten na ni phar 'dzin bde/_/de bzhin mar yang 'dzin pa bde/_/'jig rten dge sbyong 'dzin pa bde/_/de bzhin bram zer 'dzin pa bde/_/sangs rgyas rnams ni 'byung ba bde/_/de bzhin chos rnams bstan pa bde/_/dge 'dun

[\[34a.1\]]sems kyis zhi ba thob pa rnams/_/nye bar zhi zhing bde bar 'jug/_/gang zhig bde ba yangs 'dod cing /_/bde ba chung du gtong 'dod pa'i/_/brtan pas bde chung spang byas na/_/bde ba yangs pa legs par mthong /_/'jig rten 'dod bde

[\[34a.5\]]g.yo thob pa dang /_/legs par rnam par grol rnams kyi/_/'gro ba gdags su med pa yin/_/gang zhig khong na 'khrug pa med pa dang /_/gang zhig sred dang sred min las log pa/_/de dag 'jigs bral bde zhing mya ngan med/_/lhas kyang blta zhing bsam du
[\[34a.6\]]med par 'gyur/_/'di na gang dag chos mang thos pa dang /_/rtogs shing ci yang med pa kye re bde/_/skye bo skye bo'i lus la rab chags shing /_/chung zad yod pa brlag par gyur la ltos/_/'di na gang dag chos mang thos pa dang /_/rtogs shing ci yang med pa kye re
[\[34a.7\]]bde/_/skye bo skye bo'i lus la rab chags shing /_/chung zad yod pa brlag par gyur la ltos/_/skye bo ci med yon tan rtogs pa dang /_/skye bo ci yang med par gyur pa bde/_/skye bo skye bo'i sems la rab chags shing /_/chung zad yod pa brlag par gyur la ltos/_/skye
[\[34b\]]
[\[34b.1\]]bo ci med yon tan rtogs pa dang /_/skye bo ci yang med par gyur pa bde/_/skye bo skye bo'i lus la rab chags shing /_/chung zad yod pa brlag par gyur la ltos/_/gzhan gyi dbang gyur kun sdug ste/_/rang dbang yod pa thams cad bde/_/sbyor ba shin tu spang dka' ba/_/

[\[34b.4\]]gnod med pa/_/kye ma'o shin tu bde bar 'tsho/_/sha khon can gyi mi nang na/_/sha khon med par gnas pa dang /_/sha khon can nang 'khon med pa/_/kye ma'o shin tu bde bar 'tsho/_/mi thi la dag rab bsregs kyang /_/nga la ci yang tshig pa med/_/nga la gang
